RUWAN DAFA KAI 1~5
Na SUMAYYA DANZABUWA
    5
Agajiye tashigo palon nata kamar dai kullum,tana tafiya dakyar,takalmanta tacire masu uban tsini,ta watsar,sannan ta jefar da jakar kan kujera,ta cire mayafin dake jikinta ta rage kayanta,Ac ta kunna sannan tanemi waje ta kwanta duk da kuwa lokacin an fara kiran sallar laasar kuma tana ji
Bata san sanda bacci mai nauyi ya dauketa ba,Horn din motar dataji anayi shiya farkar da ita,a zabure ta farka ta kalli agogon dake makale abangon palon taga karfe 7:30 na dare,"na shiga uku banyi laasar ba,(kamar koda yaushe)gashi isha tayi,"tace arikice tareda mikewa tashige bandakin dake palon donyin alwala
Ko da ya shigo ranshi ne yabaci matuka kamar dai kullum,ganin ko ina kaca kaca ga kura kamar mutane basa rayuwa agidan,kamar ba satin daya gabata ba ya gyara gidan tsaf kafin yayi tafiya,bayan nasiha daya mata mai ratsa jiki akan tsabta,amma tasake haukata ko ina,ga kwanuka nan kan table Allah kadai yasan tun sanda suke,ga kayan ita kanta matar gida sunfi aqirga Allah kadai yasan tun sanda suke,dangin takalma mayafai da jaka ko ina,hardasu sarka,awarwaro da agoguna akan table din tsakiyar palon,bakin ciki ne da takaici suka kara turnikeshi kasancewarshi maaboncin tsabta wanda kuwa duk duniya ta shaida da hakan amma saidai kash matarshi kazama ce ta innaniha abin nata sai wanda ya gani
Lekawa kitchen yayi yaga ko ta dora wani abu saboda yasan yafada mata yau zai dawo,duk da kuwa in ya kirata ma bata dauka tun kafin yayi tafiya takejin haushinshi,don haka ya tura mata text message kuma yasan tagani, ganin babu wasu alamun girki ko shirin yin hakan ne yasashi girgiza kai,tareda fadin"Allah ya kyauta"duk da dai girkin nata bawani damuwa yayi dashi ba daman kasancewar ba iyawa tayi ba,kawai dai yana ci ne saboda ba yadda zaiyi azauna lafiya,dakuma gujewa masifarta,yace taje wajen koyar girki shi ko nawane zai biya tace ya rainata yana gaya mata magana ita tafi karfin akoya mata girki,don haka ma tadaina mishi girki inya ga dama yayiwa kanshi tunda bata birgewa,anyi wannan lamarin ana sauran kwana biyu zaiyi tafiya,"wato tana kan bakanta kenan?"yasake cewa aranshi,domin kuwa ko shi yasan yafita iya abinci,yarasa gane wane irin girman kai ne wannan ace wai mutum bai iya abu ba kuma bazai yarda bai iya ba bare har ya yarda ya karu
cikeda hanzari tafito daga bandakin,tazo ta wuceshi ta haye sama batareda ta nuna ma wai da mutum ba awajen,baki bude ya bita da kallo,shi dayayi sati daya baya gari amma irin tarbar dazai samu kenan?tunda ya tafi bata kirashi ba hasali ma idan yakirata bata dauka,anya kuwa yarinyarnan lafiyarta kalau?,ta kuwa san darajar aure bare tasan darajar miji?ya tambayi kanshi,dan karamin tsaki yaja gamida nufar nashi dakin ya shige cikeda takaici ya fada wanka
Ba abinda yake bashi mamaki kamar wannan sauyi na Farida,tabi ta chanja gabaki daya kamar ba ita ba,du du du watansu shida da aure amma gida sai kace na mahaukata,ga  uban kazanta,ya rasa wannan wace irin macece ace bazaka iya gyara inda kake zaune ba jikin ka ma sai ahankali agaskiya abin yafara isarshi kuma,tunda tadanyi tsabtar amarci shikenan kuma komai ya zama tarihi,ga girki bata iya ba hakuri kawai yake yana ci,kuma bai isa yamata nasiha ba,ita baacin gyaranta abinda takeso shi zatayi,ga babu abinda tasaka gaba sai neman kudi kamar wadda tarasa wani abu,iyayenta Allah ya rufa musu asiri,gashi shi mijinta shima babu abinda ya nema ya rasa,shikam dai yana cikin wani hali
Yunwa tafara ji bayan ta idar da sallar hakane yasata saukowa tanufi kitchen batareda tabi takan mijin nata ba,kiciniyar dafa indomie tashiga yi don itace abarda tafikwarewa akai,farkon aurensu ba abinda take dafawa sai ita tun yana shiru har ya gaji yace indomin nan fa tafara isarshi shi duk lokacin baisan ita kadai ta iya ba,tunda yayi maganar nan kuwa tafara dafa shirme saidai ya faki idonta ya waske yaje waje yaci saboda abincin bazai ciwu ba ita kadai take iyacin kayanta,ganin hakan nema yasa yakasa kawo abokanshi cin girkin nata duk nacinsu kuwa,saboda shi yasan meke wakana
Motsinta yajiyo yafito ya karasa kitchen din,tareda hadiye duk bacin ranshi,kamar koda yaushe,saboda bayason ya biye mata daga dawowarshi abubuwa suki dadi,zuwa yayi ya rungumota ta baya"my angel nayi missing dinki,ya kike"yace,banza tamishi,"shine kuma ko ki kirani kiji ya naje,naje lafiya ko ba lafiya ba shiru,babu ko dan text message,na kikkira kika ki dauka k

"yanzu dai bazaki dafa abincin daniba kike nufi ko me?"ya ktseta,"ga abinda zan dafa nan daidai cikina idan zakaci ka dafa taka ai ka iya"tace bayan tamishi nuni da indomin,baki bude ya tsaya kallonta,ganin bata wani damuba da hakan yasashi girgiza kai cikeda takaici,kamar koda yaushe cikeda  hakuri da sonta ya fito ya dauki key din motarshi ya fita neman abinda zaici
Yana fita wajen wani mai saida nama ya nufa,don tun kafin yayi aure suke zuwa shida abokinshi amininshi,kuma kasancewar madam din tashi bata iya girki ba hakan ya kara ingiza shi don kusan kullum yana cen,watarana kuma yaje wajen Hajiyarshi(mahaifiyarshi)yaci abinci,hakan baisa koda wasa yataba fada mata wani mugun abu akan faridan ba,saboda shi aganinshi kawai hakan bai kamata ba,kuma duk irin wayannan abubuwan nan sunyi wuri dayawa
wayarshi ce tafara kara alamun shigowar kira koda ya duba Bashir ne amininshi,"kana ina ne"bashir din ya tambayeshi,bayan sun gaisa,"wallahi kaganni nan ina hanyar wajen mai naman nan"yace,"ah lallai kwadayi kukeji kenan yau,kodai madam ce ta aikeka?"bashir din yasake cewa cikeda wasa ,"aa ita nama ai bawani damunta yayi ba"yace yana yar dariya,"oh to,ni da da nakira ince ka biyo,gashi madam tayi wani lafiyyayen tuwo miyar taushe nasan kuma ba abinda kake kauna kamar shi,daallah ka biyo mana amma fa karka fadawa amarya,"cewar bash,"haba dai,?dagaske to ganinan kuwa inshaallah"yace cikeda nishadi tareda kashe wayar,agaskiya yana tsaka mai wuya anya kuwa hakurinshi bazaizo yakare ba akan farida wannan wace irin macece?to ko daina sonshi tayi,?amma ai karya take tace ma batasonshi,ita da da zaa aura mata danuwanta tadagesai shi,to ai zancen rashin so ma bai taso ba,amma meyayi mata haka datake gana mishi azaba? kuma ta rainashi farat daya haka?ko don taga yanada hakuri da kau dakai?ya sha tambayarta sau ba adadi ko akwai wani abu dayake mata daya kyautawa tace bakomai idan yayi abinda yakamata zaiga daidai,ya tambayeta meye abinda yakamatan tace yafita sani,kai,shikam yafara gajiya
Yadda yaga matar bashir Amina tana tarairayar  mijin nata abun ya birgeshi sosai su dasuka ma  dan kwana biyu da aure ga girki kamar kamar me tsabar dadi,tunda yashiga gidan harya fito ko ina kamshi yake,abin dai gwanin ban shaawa,ko ina tsab tsab,tas tas,hmm shidai wato saidai yaga ana wannan abin arzikin  agidan jamaa banda gidanshi
Allahn dayayi shi yana tsananin son  miyar taushe duk wanda yasanshi yasan haka game dashi,amma dole ya hakura da ci agidanshi,domin kuwa farkon aurensu ba yadda baiyi da ita ba tayi takiyi shi duk lokacin bai gano ba,da  ya mtsa,tayi mishi wani jagwalgwalo wai miyar taushe,ashe iyawa ne batayi ba,lokacin ma yaso yaci gyaranta tanuna ita fa haka tasan anayi babu abinda tayi badaidai ba,dole ya hakura duk sanda yake shaawar tuwon sai yaje wajen hajiyarshi yaci,idan ta tambayeshi dalilin dayasa bazaije matarshi ta mishi ba sai yace nata (ita hajiyar)yake shaawa kuma yafi dadi,bai taba nuna mata cewar faridan bata iya komai ba
"Mutumina wai lafiyarka kalau kuwa duk naganka haka kayi wani iri?"bash yake tambayarshi bayan sun fito ya rakoshi mota,"haba meka gani? Ni ba abinda yake damuna lafiyata kalau,"yace,"kasan dai bama boyewa juna komai ko?kafadmin idan zan iya taimaka maka mana"yasake cewa,"dagaske karka wani damu baabinda yake damuna ras nake"yace"shine duk karame haka kuma ko?kai ko dan irin kibar angoncin nan ma shiru"cewar bash,"kufa mutane haka kuke ba dama mutum yadan rame sai ace kaza kaza nace kalau nake,to dieting nake,saida safe nabaro madam dina ita kadai dare yanayi yace"dariya sukayi duka,"to shikenan tunda kace haka,saida safe ka gaidata"sukayi sallama yashiga mota ya tafi yanata sake sake aranshi,sau dayawa idan ta kona mishi rai yakanji kamar ya rikota yadinga jibgarta baji ba gani don lamarinta saida duka,amma idan ya tuna abu daya sai yaji bazai iya ba,mace abar tausayice,abar hakuri,yakasa fadawa kowa halinda yake ciki saboda atunaninshi kamar tona asirinsu ne,kuma lokacin yayi wuri yanzu ko shekara basuyi ba,abin bazaiyi dadi ba ace an fara jin kansu,amma bakomai yasan shedan ne yakeso yashigo tsakaninsu kuma Allah bazai bashi dama ba inshallah zai cigaba da hakuri da ita yana jurewa tareda mata nasiha akoda yaushe
Koda ya dawo tadda ta yayi ta shanya hakora tana barci,yadda ya barta da kayan dai gasunan sune ajikinta,wayanda tadawo dasu ajikinta daga aiki ta cire dazatayi bacci,data tashi sallah ta maida abinta,kare mata kallo yayi ya tabbatar dai babu alamun tayi wanka,ga kwanon dataci abincin nan gefenta,wani takaicin ne  ya kamashi nacewar wato koma wanka bata damu tayi ba,ta tsabtace jikinta shida ya shafe tsahon lokaci baya gari,yasan yana matukar kaunar ta  shiyasa ma yake daga mata kafa amma kullum nema take takaishi bango yagaji dawannan halayen nata wallahi,hakkin auren nashi ma rabonda a bashi yamanta,kuma shima sau dayawa  idan yaga halin datake ciki na kazanta saiyaji kawai kwata kwata baya shaawar ya rabeta ma
Tashinta yashiga yi tareda kiran sunanta,saida yadan tabata sannan ta tashi,duk yawun bacci tana mika ga kan nan kitson Allah kadai yasan tun sanda yake," tashi inaso muyi magana"yace da ita,"mtswwww,wace irin magana ce wannan,karfe goma sha daya na dare iye?tace bayan ta kalli agogon bangon dake manne,"kai wai meyasa bakada hakuri ne bazaka iya jira ba sai gobe gari ya waye ido na ganin ido,haba mtswwwww kaii"tace tareda dan sosa jikinta,"bazan bari sai goben ba uwata yanzu nakeson muyi magana "yace a fusace,"uhm kanka akeji"tace sannan ta zame dogon skirt din jikinta yarage daga ita sai  underwear,amma fa rigar atampar na jikinta,juyawa tayi zata sake kishingida,wannan karon ma kamar ya nada mata duka yakeji don ya fuskanci ta tsananin rainashine don taga yana lallabata,amma kuma saiya yunkura zaiyi hakan sai yaga bazai iya ba hakurin dai da kauda kai shiyafi kamata,"agaskiya banajin dadin abinda kikemin farida,wai me namiki ne,?nasha tambayarki idan namiki wani laifi ne ki fadamin in gyara amma koda yaushe sai kice bakomai,yanzu fisabililahi kidubi gidan nan kigani waye zaizo yazata masu hankali ne agidan nan suke rayuwa,ji ko ina kaca kaca,shikenan dole ni zan dinga gyaran gida saboda ni na damu ko me?ke wai bakyajin komai?bakyajin kunyar ma kiyi baki suga kazantar nan?kuma kin maida wajen nan(palon)wajen kwananki kenan dakinki bashida amfani saboda ke kanki kinsan  yayi mugun dattin dabazaki iya zama ba bare har kiyi bacci wai ke wace iri ce bama kyajin komai ajikinki wai?  ga nan din shima ko ina  kaya mutum zai sauna sai ya matsar  haba farida kefa macece kuma matar aure,meyasa ne bazaki dinga tsabta ba jibeki fa tun wankan safe h

"eh lallai yusuf,"au yusuf gatsal"ya katseta baki bude don iyaka saninshi da ita bata taba bude baki ta furta sunanshi ba wato abin har yakai nan,hmm madallah,"eh nafada,lallai to sannu mahakurci,eh nace sannu uban masu hakuri wato duk kai atunaninka baiwa aka kawo maka  dazanzo indinga dawainiya dakai koh?to wallahi aa,da dabakayi auren ba waye yake maka iye?kawai saboda samun waje?bari kaji kowane dan adam fa yana bukatar hutu karfe nawa  nake shigowa gidan nan karfe nawa kuma nake fita?ina naga wannan lokacin bani dashi gaskiya,aikina yafiyemin komai  kuma bawanda zai kware wajen bada shaidar  hkan kamar kai"mata nawa ne suke aikin dayafi naki daukan lokaci amma suke tsaf tsaf dasu,wasu harda yara ma haba farida don Allah ki nutsu,wai da yaushe akayi aurennan dazamu kasance muna  samun matsala irin wanna
"nifa nasan banida wata matsala matsala daga kai ne,ana kawo yar aiki komai zai daidaita yadda kakeso,idan kuwa kace akan bakanka zaka zauna  to kuwa nima zan zauna akan nawa atoh,"wato kawo mai aikine zai sa kibar haukan dakike kishiga sahun masu hahkali kenan,to bari kiji mara kunya indai har sai an kawo miki mai aiki zaki nutsu saidai karki nutsu kiyita zama ahaka,ki zama tuburan inkinga dama amma fa kisani duk abinda ya biyo baya ke kika jawo"yace tareda mikewa sai kuma ya tsaya,"wallahi kin zalumceni,kin munafunceni dakika boyemin mugayen halayenki kika cucceni kika yaudareni na aureki,Allah ya ganar dake"yajuya yayi dakinshi,wani matsanancin kuka ta fashe dashi,"nice munafuka,azzaluma macuciya ko?to wallahi zaka sani,kuma wallahi  sai ankawo yar aikin nan sai inga mezakayi don bazai yiwu ba akasheni da raina hannu dubu ne dani?tace cikin tsiwa da masifa,ni dakai sai muga waye zaiyi nasara,inkasan wata bakasan wata ba wallahi don kuwa indai kanason zaman lafiya agidannan dole kamin abinda nakeso,"tace tareda janyo pillow tacigaba da baccinta
Lallai ma Farida wato saboda wannan banzan dalilin ne yasa takeso tamaida musu gida kamar na tababbu saboda yace bazaa kawo mai aiki ba shi dai yasan wannan haukan nata  na kazanta da rashin mutumci, ba rashin mai aiki bane kazama  ce kawai ita tun asali Allah ya sawwake yace tareda shirin kwanciya
Washegari haka ta tashi wajen karfe bakwai kasancewar sai tara take fita aiki,ko sallar asubah batayi ba bayan tashin da yayi ta mata, tun kafin ya fita masallaci har yadawo yana abu daya,hakura yayi ya kyaleta duba da wayar ta dake gefe tanata uban kara na alarm,koda wayar ta isheta janyota tayi ta kashe ta cillata gefe
A firgice ta tashi kamar ko da yaushe ta kalli agogo taga lokaci gashi gari har yayi haske,"wai wannan tsinannniyar wayar tadaina alarm ne mtswwww,yauma nayi lattin sallah"tace tareda mikewa  tayi sama, wanka tayo a bandakin da dakudi mutum  bazai iya shiga ba tsabar datti,tayi sallah sannan taciyo uwar kwalliya kamar bikinta ake,girar nan on fleek,gawani dogon takalmi,wannann shigar tata ma kullum sai sunyi fada dashi saboda shi daya cancanci yaga adonta bafa shiyake gani ba sai dai yanwaje musamman yan wajen aikinsu,akullum takan kure adaka saboda  karta fita arainta amma fa ga gida kamar kango
Turarenta shiya fargar dashi tafito tun kafin takaraso kitchen din inda yake yana hada coffeen safe,domin ba turarruka masu arha take amfani ba komanta mai tsada ne kasancewarta yar gatan iyayenta kuma tana daukan albashi sai yadda tayi dashi,kwas kwas tazo tanayi ta wuceshi a kitchen da har zai mata shiru sai kuma dai yaga gwara kada ya gajiya wajen mata nasiha,"Farida,"ya kirata tayi banza dashi tashiga laluben key din motarta a jakar jiya,biyota yayi palon yacigaba"wai sau nawa zan fada miki cewar wannan shigar dakikeyi kina fita a matsayinki na matar aure bata kamata ba?ga uban turare kin bulbula,ga wannan takalmin,ji kayan jikinki yadda suka matseki amma kika dau wannan dan karamin mayafin kika yafa,wallahi banajin dadin haka k
"yusuf kenan,da alamun dai nan gaba idan kana magana zan daina tsayawa sauraronka domin na fuskanci kai nanata zance guda daya baya maka wahala,wai wajen aikin nan a kafa nake zuwa?naga dai a motata nake waye zai ganni banda colleagues dina?kuma kowa yasan ni matar aurece,inbanda dai kanason kafara zargina nameye ne kullum saikamin zance daya?,"tace sai alokacin tagano inda ta ajiye mukullin ta tafi dauka,"To Allah ya sawwake dai kifita waje kina kwambo,kinci uwar kwallaiya ji fuskarki kamar anyi barin hoda,sai azata tsabtace dake baasan taciki  naciki ba kuwa,yanzu mintina nawa kika shafe kina neman mukullin mota?saboda tsabar rashin nutsuwa irin naki bakima san a inda kika ajiye ba Allah ya sawwake"yace bayan ya kurbi coffeen shi,duk maganar nan fa atsaye yake saboda babu wajen zama ko ina tabi tacika shi da kaya,"kowa dai yasan ni ba kazama bace"tasake cewa,tacigaba da naiman takardu acikin wata envelope,"dama mana,tunda basusan me kikeyi abayan idansu ba ba basusan wacece keba"cewar shi,"mtsww,kacigaba da fadamin duk maganar datazo bakinka,kaji ni na jawo"tace,"tabbas kuwa inda kina abinda yakamata da duk baayi haka ba ai,kazantarki ita tajawo komai,"yace,"nidai nafada kuma bazan daina fada ba wallahi bazaa kasheni daraina ba dame zanji?"Nifa kina bani mamaki,wai ke meyasa ko kunya ma  bakyaji bakuma kya kishin mijinki ma kwata kwata,nifa ina ganin kawai sona ne bakyayi,dacen dinma karya kika min har na yarda dake,wani kallo ta dago tabishi dashi,"atoh,inba haka ba wane irin shashanci ne zaisa ke dakike maaikaciya kike fita tun safe sai yamma kice zaki barwa  mai aiki ragamar gidanki  iye,wane irin sakarci ne wannan?mutane da yanzu babu wanda zaka yarda dashi kowa yazama abin tsoro?kuma bayan kinsan ni mijinki badawuri nake fita ba kuma ina dawowa da rana,aa ko kuma shikenan saboda kaunarki da maiaiki sai in fara fitar sassafe kina fita tara in biki?shikenan ni da na auro mata amma ba ita zandinga gani ba agidana sai wata cen? kicire wannan zancen daga kanki kuma kidaina maganar cewar mai aiki itace maslaha  gameda kazan tarki babu wani zancen maikaiki kazama ce ke kawai farida"yace tareda yin hanyar daki don tsayuwar ta isheshi,"kwafa tayi,taja tsaki tareda fita afisace ta tada mota maigadi ya bude mata gate ta fice kamar zata tashi sama
Kai tsaye gidan su Yusuf din ta nufa don tasan Hajiyarshi naji da ita,yanzun nan dan abu zai hadasu ita dashi ta dauki waya ta kira tafadi karya da gaskiya ita kuma hajiyan ta hau kai tazauna saboda yadda take ganin hankalinta acewarta yarinya ce mai matukar hakuri,yana zaman zamanshi sai yaga Hajiya ta kira tafara mishi fada ta inda zata shiga bata nan fa zata fita ba,haka yake hakuri akoda yaushe,bayan kuma yasha gargadinta akan bayason tadinga sako iyaye cikin yar matsalarsu bakomai bane sai anji zasu iya shirya kansu dakansu,shi datakewa laifi fa bashine mai kai kara ba sai ita
"Da sallama tashiga palon tasamu hajiyar da yan jikoki sunzo hutu suna breakfast,waje tasamu tazauna tayi kasa dakai bayan sun gaisa,sai kuma ga hawaye sharshar donma dai agaban yara ne da fashewa zatayi da kuka,"aa subhanallahi lafiya dai ko yarnan"hajiya tashiga tambayarta,"meya faru,"Hajiyar tadinga nanatawa amma ina baabinda take sai kuka mara sauti,"hajiya yusuf n""innalillahi wainna ilaihi rajiun" hajiya tafara sallalami yau ni naga takaina meya sameshi?"tace cikeda dimaucewa,"bakomai lafiyarshi kalau "tabata ansa kai tsaye,sai kuma tafara noke noke hakan ne yasa hajiyan fuskantar lallai akwai magana abakinta ,"taso mushiga daga ciki"tace da ita suka shige
"Meya faru kuma yau "hajiyar tace da ita saboda sabon da tayi da kawo kara irin nata  dukda kuwa shi yusuf din Hajiya bata tabajin yafadi wani zance mara dadi gameda matar tashi ba,har dan bugar cikinshi take amma sai yace komai kalau sun gode Allah,"inajinki meya faru""Hajiya yusuf ne yake wulakantani baji ba gani,kullum zagin dayake min daban ga cin mutumci abin baa cewa komai,babu abinda yafi batamin rai kamar zagin iyayena daya tsira kwanan nan,"tace cikin kuka,"to me kika mishi?duk abinda zakimishi yakamata ace ya zagi iyayenki?to  wai ni yaushe yaron nan yazama hakane?"hajiyar tace cikin fada,"wallahi hajiya kullum saiya zageni yacimin mutumci yagayamin magana,ba abinda yake konamin rai kamar kazama dayake kirana dashi akullum  duk kokarin danake kuwa baya gani"takarasa cikin kuka,"shi yusuf dinne duk yakeyin hakan?to lallai abinnnashi kuma yafara shallake hankali,"cewar hajiya tareda jawo wayarta zata kirashi,"hajiya basai kin kirashi ba,inda sabo ai yaci ace nasaba hakuri kawai nake ina kauda kai,"ai baa sabo da cin mutumci gwara dai in kira""Wallahi Hajiya basai kin kira ba bafa wani abu bane yasa yakemin wannan wulakancin wai kawai don nace yasamomin yar aiki tadinga taimakona h
,"au keda akan wannan dalilin nema kike tada hankali?,to yanzu  ke inbanda abinki farida meye zai gagareki agidan nan?,ni na dauka ma matan yanzu gudun mai aiki kukeyi?saboda kunce tana kwace muku miji,ki gyara gidanki ki ku
"tasake fashewa da kuka tareda katse hajiya,"wallahi hajiya bazaki gane ba,yusuf din dakika sani da bashi bane yanzu halayenshi sun sauya duka,wallahi ina iyaka bakin kokarina,haka zan tashi dasafe inyi shara inyi wanke wanke da goge goge,inyi wanki inyi girki,sannan in fita kullum ta Allah sai nayi girki gashi har ana neman a koreni daga aiki saboda latti,kullum uzuri daya nake bayarwa,duk kuwa asubancin dazanyi sai nayi latti,amma duk kokarin nan da nake baya gani haka zan gama girki ya fito yace bashi zaici ba saii na sake wani dukda kuwa yasan naa makara in nayi magana sai yace ai aiki bai fishi ba,nayi magiyar har na gaji yace ai hakkina ne in kula dashi dole in ban shiga hankalina bama saiya hana aikin"shi yusuf din?"hajiya ta katseta,gyada kai tayi alamar eh,"kuma yabi yacika gidan nan da kayanshi ko ina,idan yadawo daga aiki tundaga kofa zai fara yarda kaya,nayi nayi ya gyara yaki,haka zan dawo daga aiki banako hutawa in fara kwashe kwashe da gyare gyare sannan  inshiga inyi girki,wallahi abubuwan sunmin yawa nayi nayi ya gyara yaki nayi mishi nasihar duniyar nan yaki ji,ki taimakamin hajiya nasan ke kadai ce zaki gayamai yaji kice yabari in samo  wadda zata dinga taimakamin"takarasa cikin kuka,"hmm,lallai yusuf ai kuwa bai kyauta ba kuma yabani mamaki,ni abinda yake daure min kai shine chanjawarshi cikin kankanin lokaci,amma bakomai zanyiwa tufkar hanci inma wasune suke zugashi duk zanyi maganin komai"hajiya tace"don Allah hajiya ki agaza min ki taimakeni don gab nake da

RUWAN DAFA KAI 6~10Na SUMAYYA DANZABUWA
Cikin hanzari yagama shiri ya nufi gida duk atsorace,tunanin ko ba lafiya ba,koda ya isa  motar farida yagani a harabar gidan,hakan ne ya tabbatar mishi da dalilin kiran hajiya,girgiza kai yayi kawai tareda fadin Allah shi kyauta kamar koda yaushe
A kuryar daki yasamesu hajiya nata mata aikin sannu tayi shame shame agadon sirika,gaishe da hajiya ya fara ta ansa ciki ciki kamar an mata tilas,domin kuwa babu abinda ta tsana arayuwar duniya kamar taga namiji yana wulakanta mace,harta kai ga yana fada mata mugayen maganganu gashi shi yusuf nashi lamarin farida tace mata harda zagi,dole tadau mataki, "so kake ka kasheta kenan?wato wai kaima kazama namijin duniya ko? to wallahi ka kiyayeni ka guji bacin raina yaushe kazama hakane ni wai?ko wasune suke zugaka?iye?ta inda hajiya take shiga bata nan take fita ba shi mamakine kawai ya isheshi,ya tsaya kallonta, cikeda rashin fahimtar zancen,bata jira ya tambaya bama ta zayyane mishi duk yadda sukayi da faridan,"ya ilahi,wallahi karya takeyi duk abinda ta fada babu wanda zan iyayi aciki ke kanki kinsanni hajiya banma san ya akayi kika yarda da ita ba y
" rufemin  baki anan,baga  alamu nan  ba nagani yarinya duk ta rame saboda kana neman hallaka
,"wayyo Allah cikina Hajiya ki taimakeni"tace tana murkususu a gado,"gashinan tsabar wahala datakesha tun dazu take amai dama kai nake jira  maza dauketa mu tafi asibiti"Hajiya tace,"yanzu ni shikenan bazakiji nawa bangaren ba na zan
"wayyo Allah na zan mutu"tasake kwala kara don kar yatona mata asiri,don har tafarajin yana cewa idan karya yake mata  hajiya  tabishi suje aga yadda tazamar da gidan,ita kuwa bazataso  haka ba,"banason wani zance maza dauketa mutafi kana bata lokaci"ba yadda ya iya,haka ya mata daukan jarirai dama ba wani nauyine da ita ba ta lafe,suka tafi asibiti harda hajiyan
Gwaje gwaje aka musu suka  zauna jiran sakamako,Hajiya tanata mita tanamai fada ba yadda baiyi ba wajen ganin ya fuskantar da ita ga gaskiyar lamarin takijinshi,saboda farida bata taba rashin mutumci agabanta,zuciyarshi nata kuna ga hajiya taki ta daina mishi fada,kememe takiyarda da zancenshi,ana cikin hakan ne likita yazo musu da albushir din  tana dauke da juna biyu na tsahon wata uku
Murna awajen yusuf abin sai wanda yagani har yamanta ma da bacin ran dayake ciki,sakamakon son yaya da Allah ya dora mishi,ita kuma uwar gayyar sai wani yatsine yatsine take dukda kuwa itama tana cikin dinbin farinciki amma wai dole ne anuna mai fa har yanzu fushin akeyi dashi,hajiya itama tayi tata murnar,taji dadi sosai dukda kuwa ba dan yusuf bane zai zame mata jika na farko amma ko acikin yayan nata yakasance abin kaunarta saboda halayyarshi ta kwarai,"zaku iya tafiya,sai dai a kula da ita sosai don Allah,kekuma malama farida duk sanda kikaji wani abu da ba daidai ba kar abata lokaci a garzayo,zamu baki wasu yan magunguna sai  akiyaye  shansu,congratulations Allah ya raba lafiya"doctor  yace da yusuf tareda mika mishi hannu
"Wannan abu yayi,to kadaiji abinda yace,gashi agabanka dai akayi,bawai labari ka samu ba,kar inji kar in gani kada ka kuskura  yau ta kare batareda ka samo mata yar aikin nan ba don idan da kanada  uzuri yanzu babu dolene tasamu kulawa dakyau cikin fari ne,"cewar Hajiya tareda karasawa inda suke,ta kwashi takalman faridan,dukansu kallo suka bita dashi,"meye ka tsaya kana kallona daukota mana,ai yanzu kulawa  ta musammamn ita take bukata,maxa adaukota"tace tareda juyawa tayi hanyar fita,"amma hajiya ni in,
"kai wai yaushe kazama hakane ashe dai duk gaskiya ta fada zakazo kanamin musu gashi nagani agabana,"zai sake magana ta dakatar dashi,dole ya dauko ta ta lafe harda mishi gwalo ranta kal cikeda jin dadin taci nasara,zakuma tacigaba da horonshi son ranta
Baiwani damu ba don wannan labari mai dadi ya shafe dukkanin laifukanta a wajenshi
Haka suka shige mota dukkaninsu hajiya da ita suna baya ta sheme kanta a cinyar hajiya,tana ta mata sannu ahaka suka karasa gida,tana shiga ta sake shemewa agado,"toh kadaiji komai banason inyita maimaita zance daya,aje maza asamo mata mai taimaka mata ni don bansan wanda zan sa ya samo bane shiyasa datuni nasa ankawo","hajiya ni abinda nakeso ki gane shine cikin nan fa baiwani dade ba bare ya fara wahalarwa ni aganina yanzu dai daga ni sai ita agida babu abinda zai gagareni wallahi don dai shara da wanke wanke,kuma itama ai zaifi kyau ace tana dan motsa jik
"kayya!kanaso kadinga bata min rai naga  alama wato"walahi bahaka bane hajiya ka

"Ranki ya dade buri dai ya cika koh?"yace da ita tareda murmushi,yar dariya tayi cikeda jin dadin cin nasara "eh mana to ai dama kaine kaki zaman lafiya,daanyi hakan tuntuni ai da duk abubuwan dasuka faru basu faru ba"au hakane?Shiyasakika zabi ki hadani da uwata ta hanyar sharga mata karairayi akan abinda ban aikata ba ko,?To ai shikenan yayi kyau tunda  kin samu burinki ya cika sai acigaba da abin kirki adinga kyautatawa miji"yace bayan yakoma kusa da ita ya zauna,"Allah  inasonki farida kema kinsani,dabana sonki da wayannan abubuwan dakike aikatamin bazan daukesu ba kin sani ko?amma duk hakurin danakeyi,bakya gani, kika zabi ki wahalar dani akan abinda baikai yakawo ba,wallahi kin fiya fitina"yace cikeda kaunar ta"inasonka nima kuma kasani amma kaine badama ince kaza sai kace bahaka ba kuma duk abinda nayi ban iya ba,"tace cikin shagwaba"ni bacewa nayi baki iya ba kawai inkin danyi kuskure ne nake kokoarin ganin nadan gyara mikinamma ke bakyason hakan,to yanzu  dai komai so nake ya wuce,mai aiki dai kisa akawomiki ita,Allah yadaidaita,shikenan?"Amin tace tareda kara shigewa jikinshi"sai kuma gyaran jikin nan don Allah don Annabi  kidinga gyara jikinki,wannan dai ai ba aikin da me aiki zatayi bane ba dai ko?wanka daya arananyamiki kadan amatsayinki na matar  aure gashi aiki kike zuwa bafa agida kike ba,yanzu jibi gashin kanki fa"yace tareda zame dankwalin dake kanta Hajjaju"ni zanje masallaci,"yace sannan ya tashi ya fita
Sai wajen laasar suka fara shirin tafiya Hajiya tace  su tafi da motar faridan inyaso sai tasa Malam Hamisu driver yakawo mishi  tashi,sallama sukayi  bayan tamusu nasiha mai ratsa jiki sanan tasake jaddadawa kada fa taji kada tagani ayi hakuri azauna lafiya
Abinda yasa Hajiyar Yusuf take nan nan da farida shine,ita azamaninta bata samu hakan ba daga gurin tata sirikar banda hantara da kyara babu abinda tasamu sai wahala,haka shima babansu Yusuf din bata tsira ba a wajenshi,duka da zagi babu wanda bataci ba,har su yusuf din suka girma,ta nemi da araba auren bazata iya ba,Dakyar aka samu yasaketa,yace kuma ta tafi da yayanta shi bazai iya ba,dole ta tafi dasu gida,cen gidan ma zaman kunci akayi domin kuwa mahaifiyarta ta dade da rasuwa sai matar babanta,inda tadinga gallaza mata itada yaranta,kuma baban bai isa yace komai ba saboda sai abinda tace akeyi
Bayan rabuwar auren da kimanin shekara daya,Babansu yusuf ya rasu
Haka Hakiya tacigaba da zaman hakuri agidan baban nata,har dai Allah yasa Wata rana wani danuwan mahaifinta yazo yaga halin da ake ciki,tausayinta da yaranta ne yakamashi yasa ya tafi dasu duka gidanshi,inda yamaidata karatu tayi nisa,yaranta suma  suka dan kara girma,tana gamawa bata dade ba tasamu aiki albashin kuwa ba laifi,hakan ne yasata nemo gidan dazasu zauna itada yaranta,sakamakon gajiyawa da matar danuwan mahaifin mata tafara nunawa itama
A takaice dai su yusuf da yanuwanshi biyu,Asmau,da Aisha,wayanda duk sun dade da aure harda yaransu,mahaifiyarsu itace uwarsu itace ubansu,ita ta girmar dasu,da dadi ba dadi Har Allah yasa suka kawo iyanzu,Allah ya buda musu sunyi Arziki Alhamdulillah har suna taimakawa wasu
Idan farida tana mishi Rashin kunya tana rashin mutumci yaji kamar ya daketa sai ya tuno da mahaifiyarshi wancen lokacin,yadda mahaifinsu yake dukanta agabansu basu isa su tare mata ba kasancewarsu yara,don dukansu basuda wata tazara,saidai su zauna suyita kuka,hakika tuna wasu abubuwan har yanzu idan yayi yakanyi  kwalla
Itama hajiya ta bangarenta kusan hakane,don ganin irin wahalar datasha abaya ne yasa bata sassautawa duk namijin datagani yana wulakanta mace,musamman ma yusuf da farida take kawo mata karya da gaskiya akanshi,saboda tasan yadda abin yake dakadan dakadan ake farawa,kuma yusuf yaso ya hana farida aiki da farko tace karta kuma ji,ba daidai bane mace tazauna bata komai koda yaushe saidai tajira mai miji zai bata,hakan lallai akwai gajiyawa
Wayannan dalilai su suka saka Yusuf kara kaimi wajen hakuri da farida aganinshi watarana sai labari duk abinda take zata daina,duniyar ba komai bace,amma idan yace zai sako duka ko cin mutumci bazata taba yafe mishi ba,kuma bazaiso abin yakai har yayansu sugani ba,zasu tsaneshi kuma hakan zai mishi ciwo kwarai dagaske
Ai suna kama hanyar tafiya gida ta kira kawarta Samira abokiyar aikinta,tace maza maza akawo mata yarinya irin wadda sukayi magana,kar awani bata lokaci,"madam kyadai bari gobe ko?yanzu ai dare yafarayi" yace da ita,"toh naji gobe gobe don Allah kar awuce gobe,eh ina nan inajira tace sannan ta kashe wayar ta turawa samira text kamar haka"muna tare ne shi shiyasa  banason inyi magana agabanshi kar yaji nawani damu dashi irin sosai dinnan,har yaji ina cewa banason mai kaza kaza,kinsan yada mukayi dake sammy banason yarinya irin yar karamar nan,nafison yar matashiya,kinsanni dai,bakuma nasan tsohuwa,mummuna nakeso yar lukuta baka,irin wayanda suka horu da aikin nan?suka sha noman doya,ina fatan kin gane harda saka emoticon din dariya mai hawaye()yadda babu yadda zaayi ma inyi fargaba bare inyi tunanin har zai iya kallonta ta birgeshi asamu matsala,goben in Allah yakaimu akawota don Allah nagode,ta tura mata
"Wai mekiketayi ne awayar nan sai magana nake kinyi shiru"yace,don tunda ta gama waya yake janta da hira tana uhmm aa,hakan ne ya tabbatar mishi dacewar dole da abinda take,"bakomai fa kawai ina dan replying messages ne","ok,ke inbanda abinki kyace mai aiki tazo yau?kin manta halin da gidan nan yake ciki?me kike tunanin zai faru idan tazo tagani,kina ganin bazata dinga miki wani kallo ba ta rainaki?"yace cikeda wasa,"to wane raini kuma itada tazo aiki ai don ta gyara aka kawota koba haka ba,"hmm hakane kam madam"yace,don bai fiyason sudinga jan zance ba,tafiya musu kullum itace akan daidai yanzunnan idan aka tsawaita magana sai ta nemi tayi mishi rashin kunya,saida suka biya wani wajen  abinci yamusu takeaway sannan suka wuce gida
Wai ita ko damuwa ma batayi mijinta yadinga cin  abincin waje,har aje ma da ita asiya su cinye tare ko kishi babu,haka zata zauna tadinga santi tana yabon girkin agabanshi bako kunya,bare damuwa,bata damu taga ta iya ba ma,yace ta je akoya mata,ko ya samo akoya mata har gida tace ya rainata yaci mata mutumci,hmm tana tunanin ahaka zasu dawwama kenan?,muje zuwa
Daren ranar dai gwanin ban shaawa sai wanda ya gansu,tare sukayi aikin suka gyaggyara  komai aka saka turaren wuta,saboda kada mai aiki tazo taga aika aikar matar gida,cikeda so da kauna suka dinga komai dukda kuwa ita ko rabi batayi ba,shine yayi komai,sai shemewa take wai ita mai ciki,dayayi magana yace kaza sai tace agabanshi fa likita yace tadaina aiki,dole yadingaallabata yana rarrasinta hardai suka kwanta,su farida anyi wankan dare anyi kwalliya ansha kayan bacci masu daukar hankalin miji,kamar ba ita ba,atakaice dai sun raya wannan dare,domin kuwa yusuf yayi farincikin daya dade baiyi ba
Da asubah shine yafara tashi kamar koda yaushe,wanka yashiga yayi yayo alwala,yafara aikin tashin gimbiyar,(haka take kamar matacciya idan tana bacci,)dakyar yasamu ta dan motsa,sannan yafara mata  magiya akan idan tanayiwa Allah kada ta koma bacci yadawo yaga tayi sallah,sama sama tadinga bashi ansa don dai tasamu yarabu da ita

RUWAN DAFA KAI 1 - RUWAN DAFA KAI - Wattpad
RUWAN DAFA KAI 21-25Na SUMAYYA DANZABUWA
Tunda Naomi takarfafawa gloria gwiwa  akan jan hankalin yusuf gloria ta dage wajen ganin tacimma burinta,dama idan Farida ta fita dasafe su biyu take bari agidan,kuma hakan bai taba damunta ba don batada wata fargaba,ga  yusuf sai wajen sha daya yake fita, hakane yabawa gloria damar saka matsatstsun kayanta datazo dasu,wayanda tafara sawa tun farkon zuwanta kafin farida ta hanata a tunaninta ko zata birge yusuf har ya kamu da sonta amma ina kamar  kullum idanunshi kara dakushewa  suke suna makancewa in tana guri
A kullum takan matse jiki gata dama  ba laifi a dire take,tanada  duk wasu abubuwa/surori na jikin mace dazasu iya jan hankalin namiji fuskartata  cedai sai ahankali don tubarakallah Allah yamata muni,daba don muninta ba Allah kadai yasan mazan dazasu mace akanta,a koda yaushe Farida tana barin gidan zata shige daki ta shiryo taci uwar kwalliya  saita daidaici lokacin fitowar yusuf saita zo ta zauna a palon bayan zaman palon ma farida ta hanata,amma matukar bata gidan abinda taga daama takeyi,ko sau daya yusuf bai taba nuna wa ma wai yana ganinta ba bare yasan wai metake sakawa ajikinta,ko metaje nufi,tunda shidai bawai abinci zai tsaya ci ba idan ya sauko zai fita bakuma zama yake ba a palon,kama hanyarshi kawai yake ya fita,duk da kuwa a kullum bata gajiya saita gaisheshi ta mishi adawo lafiya amma ko ansata bayayi tunda ya lura da taketakenta amma hakan bai taba sawa ta gajiya ba,sannu dazuwa ne dai bata samuwa domin matar gida tana nan kuma tasha ja mata kunne indai mijinta yana gida karta dinga ganin ko gifcinta indai ba ita ta kirata ba
Duk abinnan daa ake shima yusuf din ko sau daya bai taba yiwa farida zancen ba na cewar wai gashi gashi abinda gloria takeyi idan ta fita saboda bashida wannan lokacin ba abu bane daya shafeshi,tunda ai bashi ya kawota ba,bakuma zamanshi take ba,zaman farida takeyu, harkar ta ita ta shafa shi babu ruwanshi dukda sai shiyake bada kudin aikinta,baima  zama lallai ma ta yarda ba idan ya fada mata halin daake ciki,yasan hakinta zata iya cewa saboda bayason zamanta ne zai mata sharri,shikuwa yanzu akan gloria dai yariga yagama magana don babu abinda zaisa ya sake  tada wani zance kuma,kansu akeji daga ita har uwar dakin nata

Duk abubuwan dasuka faru akan idon gloria,ita babu abinda take fata kamar ace farida da yusuf sun rabu maana ya saketa kawai in yaso ita ta aureshi,don har tafara jin alamun cin nasara,batayi wani wata wata ba takira naomi ta labarta mata komai inda ta kara karfafa mata gwiwa akan karta sarara har saita cimma burinta kuma zata tayata addua itama akan mutuwar auren
Koda yusuf ya karasa daki alwala yayi yafara jero nafiloli,bayan ya idar ya zauna yadinga jero adduoi,don indai ibada ne badaga nan ba,akwaishi da ilimin addini mashaallah,adduoin yadinga jerowa akan idan aurenshi da farida akwai alkhairi aciki Allah ya daidaitasu ya sa ta nutsu don yana tsananin sonta bazai yaudari kanshi ba halayenta ne bayaso idan babu alkhairi Allah ya musanya mishi da abinda yafi alkhairi don hakika yasan zaman dayayi da ita ba karamin hakuri yayi ba yakai zuciyar shi nesa ba abu bane dakowa zai iya,ahankali yadinga samun sassauci daga kunar dazuciyarshi kemishi,har hakan yasashi dauko wayarshi don ya kirata ya tabbatar dai lafiyarta kalau,amma ko daya duba watsapp yaganta online saiya fasa kiran,saboda hakan ya tabbatar mishi dacewar lallai tana cikin koshin lafiya,hotonsu ma dake kan dpnta tacire,bayan babu yadda baya fama da ita akan tadaina saka hotonsu a social media takiji amma yau saboda tana jin haushinahi gashi don kanta tacire,murmushi kawai yayi cikeda mamakin irin karfin halinta,sannan ya fara shirin kwanciya,hankalinshi kwance yake komai don yasan dole gida ta tafi kuma ma besides shi fa tayiwa laifin nanma amma itace mai zakewa,yasan ko zaiyi bikonta saiya ja ajinshi ya bata mamaki,ko dayake ma indai wannance ba lallai hakan ya dameta ba,wata zuciyar tace dashi,haka ya zauna yadinga tunane baisan sanda bacci yayi awon gaba dShi ba
Washegari dasafe yana saukowa yayi arba da gloria taci uwar kwalliya ko kallonta baiyi ba kamar dai kullum,tazo yay don karfin hali harda tararshi a bakin stairs wai zata karbi jakarshi takaimishi mota,bayan ta gaisheshi bai ansa ba,"ke,respect yourself,kifita harkata"yace cikin sanyayyiyar muryarshi,wani dadi taji don ko bakomai ya kulata,har ya kai bakin kofa saikuma ya tsaya,"ki tabbata kin bar gidannan kafin in dawo saboda ba zamana kikeyi ba,wadda kike zamanta itama ta tafi duk sanda ta dawo ta dawo dake,and I dont want to repeat myself,kada na dawo naganki"yace batareda ya juyo ba yajuya ya fita,"wannan mai yake nufi?korata ma yake ban cimma burina ba?hmm,ai kuwa ba inda zanje saidai duk abinda zaiyi yayi"tafadi hakan afili,"aa gloria he sounded so serious kuma wannan zai iya miki dukan tsiya ko yasa,ki tafi din kamar yadda yadda yace tunda kinasonshi idan matar tashi tadawo saiki dawo,bakomai kiyi hakuri"wata zuciyar tace mata,dakinta takoma ta kwashi yan abinda zata kwasa ta tafi
Kai tsaye office din bash yanufa, inda ya bashi labarin duk abinda yafaru kamar yadda yayi alkawari amma fa saida yadan sassakaya bakin halin farida musamman akan abokananshi da matansu don yasan tabbas idan bash din yaji bazaiji dadi ba saidai kawai ya kauda kai,kuma dai tunda har yanzu yana ganin mutumcin farida bazaiso yafadi abinda zai zubar mata da mutumci ba,tunda matarshi ce har yanzu,bazai iya tona mata asiri haka kawai ba,gwara tadinga nuna irin bakin halinta dakanta tunda halinta ne,hakika bash din ya jinjina lamarin sanin halin abokin nashi ba daga baya ba indai ta fannin hakuri ne,shiyasa duk abubuwan dayafada yana jurewa bai waniyi mamaki ba,"kacigaba da hakuri yusuf amma ni dai ina ganin gwara kabita d
"kaji na ma rantse ko,to Wallahi yadda tasa kafa ta fita ban koreta ba haka zatasa ta dawo,indai har saina daukota ne to kuwa tayita zama

Bayan tagama shirin tafiya aiki,tazauna breakfast ga komai nan anshirya mata,taba zaune tanaci hankalinta kwance da alamun babu abinda ya dameta,mama tajiyo ta budo kofar shigowar palon,"wannan turaren kuma fa?"maman tace bayan ta fito taji palon ya cika da kamshin turare,kamar anyi bari,tabbas abin ya wuce hankali,koda ta duba kan dining table farida tagani da alamun kuma dai ita kadaice a palon turaren nata ne itace ta fesashi,shiru tayiwa maman kamar bataji taba tacigaba dacin abincinta,don tasan dama sai tayi magana,"wai yaushe mama zata dinga ganin abu ko taji tayi shiru ne?"tace aranta,haka ta kyale maman tacigaba da magana batareda ta bata ansa ba har saida ta karaso inda take, sai lokacin ta dago kanta ta kalleta"ina kwana mama"tace tareda cigaba da latsa wayarta tana cin abinci,"haba farida,yanzu fisabilillah hakan ya dace kenan?Kina nufin kicemin haka kike fita kullum da wannan uban turaren kina mace?matar aure?wai meyasa yaran nan kukeson kudinga jawa kanku magana ne ku kuma jamin?yanzu duk wanda yaganki yaji kina wannan uban kamshin bacewazaiyi bakida ilimi ba bakisan hukuncin yin hakan ba a addinance?baki kumasan ciwon kanki ba jibi fuskarki fa?da wannan uwar kwaliyar kike fita kullum kije wajen aikin duk da maza?ko shakka babu nasan wannan yana daga cikin irin dalilan dayasa kika samu matsala da mijinki,domin kuwa duk namiji mai hankali da nutsuwa dayasan meyakeyi yake kishin matarshi bazai so ta fita ahaka ba kuma na tabbata yasha miki magana tunda kuwa yusuf din ai ba shashasha bane irinki,walahi nayi imanin zalumtar yaron nan kikeyi k
"wai don Allah sai kidinga cewa wai ina zalumtar shi,ni duk abubuwan dayamin wai baki gani ba?,yanzu kin gwammace kidinga fifita wani akannyarki,haba mama?yanzu har namijin dazai sa hannu yadaki mace shine wani abin damuwa?tace cikeda mita "wai yaushe zaki fara min kallon yarki ne don Allah?"bansani ba,wato ni kike gayawa haka kina titsiyeni?"saboda inaso in ceceki?to yayi kyau kiyi abinda kikaga dama kinji idan kin tashi wanki kidinga wanki da ruwan turare shine zaki birgeni"maman tace tareda juyawa ta rabu da ita,"kiyi hakuri ni ban fadi hakan don in bata miki ba"tace sannan ta tashi ta kama hanyar fita batareda tagama cin abincin ba sai don gudun yin latti,bata goge fuskar ba ko ta chanja kayan masu turaren haka tazo ta wuce ta gaban maman
Kallo kawai maman ta bita dShi ta girgiza kai"wato dai bata isa da yayan data haifa ba,saboda mahaifinsu ya bata mata su,to Allah dai yasani ta rabu da iyayenta lafiya bata taba bata musu ba barema tace dama Alhaki kwikiyone ko sakayya take gani kawai dai tasan cewar dan yaune ka haifeshi baka haifi halinshi ba Allah ya shiry yasa sugane gaskiya shine adduarta agaresh a kullum
Yau kimanin sati daya kenan da dawowar farida gida amma ga mamakinta yusuf kememe yaki nemanta,ko a watsapp yaki kulata bare ayi zancen kiran waya ko tura sakon text message,saidai taganshi online,ko taga yayi updating status da alamun kuma baya cikin kunci bayan ita gatanan tarasa indazata saka kanta,bawai dadin zaman gidansu bane bataji amma kawai tana bukatar mijinta akusa da ita,gashi shikuma yana nuna mata fa babu shi acikin wannan lamarin na shashancinta, da alamun dai ita kadai take kidanta take rawarta,shi habkalinshi a kwance yake,da taji wayarta tayi kara take dauka a dari tana tunanin ko shine amma ina bashida niyyar kira,tabbas tasan ita tayi mishi laifi tasan itace baakan gaskiya ba,amma so take dole saiyazo ya bata hakuri yadda yasaba,ko dayake ma to akan me ma zata bashi hakuri,?bayan ya fifita matan abokananshi akanta?mtsww taja tsaki a fili cikeda takaici,idan ta tuna abinda yamata sai haushinshi ya kamata,mtsw tasake jan tsaki "kanshi ake ji"tace tacigaba da harkokinta amma fa duk abinda zatayi hankalinta nakanshi,sai yayita fado mata,tasan tana missing dinshi sosai so take kawai taganshi ko taji muryarshi,amma kuma inaaa,dole taja aji,wato in ta kirashi ita tama damu dashi kenan yaji dadin rainata wato hmm zai bushe
,zancen zuci take amma tana tsaki afili,"ke kuma lafiyarki zakisa mutane agaba kina tsaki idan yi zakiyi sai kishiga daki"cewar safina,"shikenan tsakinma banida ikon yi?ko kuwa bakinki ne?"ta hayayyako mata dama ta mugun rainata ga safinan itama bata jan girmanta dama haka sukaso su fara rigima kafin mama tashiga tsakani"ai bakuga komai ba tukun,tunda dai haka kuka zabarwa kanku,din Allah ku kashe kanku kafin inshiga in fito,shine zaku birgeni inga karahen haukanku,sakarlaru"tace sannan tashige,cikeda jin haushin safeena Farida ta tashi tayi hanyar daki tana tafiya dakyar,saboda cikin ta ya fito sosai
A Gaskiya Itafa zaman gidan nan yafara isarta wallahi gashi dai ita ta hada komai tayiwa mijinta kazafi da sharri akan abinda bai aikata ba gashi ta shafa mishi bakin fenti a idon yan gidansu musamman mahaifinta don abin bai bashi dariya ba kwata kwata,tana tsammanin zaizo bikonta yabata hakuri amma shiru,ga ba damar ita ta kirashi ya rainata to wai ita yazatayi idan yace ya saketa ne?wai meye mafita ne,?kai tasan fa tana masifar son mijinta ita wai me ma yakaita ne ?ta dai debo ruwan dafa kanta kawai tace aranta
"Wai yaron nan har yanzu bai biyo sahun yarinyar nan bane?"Abba ya jefowa mama tambaya,"ah inda ya biyo ai da kaji,kuma ma akan mezai biyota bayan ita takamo hanya ta taho"cewar mama,"nifa kina bani mamaki wai meyasa zaki dinga magana hakane,akan meye bazata dawo gida ba kinajin yanaci mana mutumci yanadukanta wato so kike tazauna ya kasheta kenan ga ciki ajikinta ko kuwa dai me kike nufi ?"ya hayayyako,"ko daya,kawai dai inason in fuskantar dakai cewar batada gaskiya kwata kwata tunda kuwa zaman datasaka kanta takeyi agidannan kake kuma goya mata baya a takure take inda yaron nan ne da laifi(yusuf)yaci ace yabbiyo sahun nata duk rashin khnyarshi kuwa,to a
"to ai kuwa indai bazaizo ya nemi sulhu ba ya bada hakuri auren nan angamashi tunda shi bashida mutumci yarinyar yau satinta daya agida ga ciki amma ya kyaleta,bai damu ma da halin datake ciki ba,naga ta koma gidan nashi wallahi baisanni bane don idan yakuskura yabari aka kara kwana biyu kwana biyu kacal wallahi baizo ba saina aika mishi ya aiko mata da takardarta ni tunda ni tazamewa dole bazan gaji da ganinta ba inason kayata"ya tashi ya fita a fusace batareda yajira mai maman zatace ba don zantukanta bata mishi rai suke,duk abinnan daake a kunnen farida,"shi kuwa Abba yadau Abinnan dazafi,yana nufin indai yusuf baizo dakanshi ba bazan koma dakina ba kenan?tab ashe kuwa da alamun nima zan cigaba dazama don yadda nake ganin alamu bazuwa zaiyi ba,na kaishi bangon dayake fada,idan baizo ba nanda kwana biyu a aikomin takarrdata?tab,nifa bacewa nayi banason mijina bafa,shikenan daga mundan sami matsala maimakon a lallabani in koma kuma sai adinga zancen saki"tace aranta cikeda mamakin irin son da mahaifinsu yake musu dahar zai dinga jure kashe musu aure wai don sunce ana musu ba daidai ba
"To Ko dai zuwa zatayi tasameshi dakanta tafada mishigaskiyar lamura?don mama ba abinjibace tariga ta ganota,tasan gaskiyar lamarin,kai anya kuwa zata iya?me Abba zai dauketa kenan?makaryaciya?kuma yanzu idan nagasken yazo yafaru fa wazai saurareta?kai dasake dole tayi tunani kafin lokaci ya kuremata tazo tana danasani, don duk abinda zatayi yakamata ace tayi shi taakanin yau da gobe kar waadin da Abba ya dauka yacika

Nan farida tacigaba da kitsa sharri kala kala,sannan tagayawa Hajiya tunda yusuf ya koreta bai bi sahunta ba,hasalima ko kiranta baiyi ba,ita tadinga kira ma tabashi hakuri baya dauka,sai hakuri aka bata agida tadawo,ita kam takusa gajiya da hakuri,rarrashinta Hajiya tacigaba dayi saboda yadda take kuka kamar ranta zai fita,ana cikin haka Yusuf Yayi sallama

"ya bazaka ganta haka ba,duk waye silan zamanta hakan iye?yusuf nagaji da nanata zance daya fa naga alamun dai so kake musaka kafar wando daya dakai",Ta inda Hajiya take shiga bata nan take fita ba,shi abin ma yadaure mishi kai,"Allah ya huci zuciyarki amma bana fatan Allah ya nuna min wannan lokacin,idan babu damuwa zanso naji dalilin kiranki Hajiya don wallahi Duk abubuwan dakike fada bangane ko daya ba daga ciki,ga Farida tana kuka kekuma kinata fada,ko nasake miki wani abinne?"yace tareda kallon faridan,shiru tamishi ta kalli kasa,don indai agaban Hajiya ne nunawa take babu wanda ya iya biyayya sama da ita ga mijinta baya fada taja bare tayi musu,"naji duk ahinda ka aikata ai,wato dai kana nufin ban isa ba,duk zancen mai aikin nan da aka dinga yi anan wajen,don inda wajen nan yana magana da ya bada shaida nifa da kai mukayi yarjejeniya akan kada inji kada in gani amma,ashe ban isa ba,"Hajiya tace cikin fada,"nifa mai aikin nan ba korarta mayi ba"yace sannan yayi shiru,"to me kayi?ka kori matar gida sai kaga ya dace ka kori kowa kenan kazauna kai kadai saboda ana takura maka ko ba haka bane?"hajiya tace ckeda fada,"babu wannan niyyar azuciyata kuma ni babu wanda nakora,ban kori farida ba Hajiya ita takama hanya tayi tafiyarta gida,tabarni da mai aikinta nikuma tun farko kowa yasan bason yarinyar nan nake ba,kuma babu abinda take min shine nace to taje duk sanda uwardakin nta ta dawo ta dawo da ita shine kawai abinda nasan ya faru,"yace,batareda yafadi babban dalilin dayasa yace glorian ta tafi ba,wanda kuwa inda faridan tasan da haka dabatayi giginyimishi hauka ba har tace zata kawoshi kara,"nidai ba haka tace min ba cewa tayi kai ka koreta ko bahaka kika cemin ba?"Hajiya ta watso mata tambaya,kuka ta fashe dashi,"Ni dai babu abinda zance tunda burinka a kullum shine kuntata min Allah saiya sakamin tace cikin kuka"hmm lallai farida harke kike zancen sakayyya?to kuwa kinyi babban kuskure don kuwa babu wanda ya cancanci sakayya kamar
koda yake ma shikenan dai,"dama mana ai dole kace haka,"Cewar Hajiya shiru kawai yayi don yasan idan yace zai zauna yafadwa hajiya komai gameda farida hawan jininta zai iya tashi shikuwa bazaiso haka ba acigaba da tafiya Ahaka Sakayyar datake ikirarai tana nan tafe
Ana cikin wannan yanayi daya daga cikin yayyen yusuf din Aisha tazo,sakamakon zuwan dasukayi gari bikin kanwar mijinta,dukansu ita da Asmau Babbar yayarsu baa gari suke aure ba,ita a Abuja take amma suna da gida a Kano,Asmau kuma tana Germany shiyasa haduwa take wahala
"Banason nasake jin zance irin wannan,nagaji daji,kuzauna lafiya auren nan ko shekara baayi ba amma kullum matsalar yau daban ta gobe aban wallahi banajin dadi,Allah yabaka nutsatsiyar mace,amma kana nuna rashin godiyarka,yusuf ka rike matarka hannu bibbiyu kadinga mutum tata kema farida kicigaba da hakuri da mijinki kina girmamashi,banaso in sake jin wani zance makamancin wannan,sai kuma lamarin mai aikin nan tunda na fuskanci shine ummul abaisin komai ki hakura da ita tunda yadage,naga kuma da alamun zamanta agidan shike harzuka abubuwa,zansa asamomiki wata,burina akulllum inga ana zaman lafiya a aure ana kare hakkin juna"Hajiya mai aikin nan batada laifi aduk abubuwan nan,kuma wallahi a halin danake ciki ita kadaice ta dace dani,saboda ta iya aiki gashi yau na dauki hutu daga aiki har saina haihu zan koma nariga nagama gajiya ba lallai bane idan an tashi samowa asamo irinta wadda ta iya komai"to shikenan bakomai,n
"Kiyi hakuri da abinda zance Hajiya,"cewar yusuf wanda tunda suka fara zancen baisa musu baki ba,"Gidan nan dai gida nane,kuma ke matata tace ko na isa da ke,"yafadi hakan yana mai kallon farida,"to nace wannan yarinyar bazata cigaba damiki aiki ba kisamo duk wadda zaki samo amma banda ita,Hajiya kiyi hakuri idan zancen bai miki dadi ba,amma wannan karon bazan iya ba,"wannan irin tsana har ina?ni na taba ganin abu irin haka?"Ba tsana bace inada dalilina nayin hakan,ban hanata kawo mai aiki ba takawo duk wadda takeso, amma waccen ce bazata dawomin gida ba"yace tareda fuskantar farida,wadda tunda ya fara zancen ta sunkiyar dakai saboda tsananin biyayya,"hmm anya kuwa yaron nan bashine mai gaskiya ba?nafasan halin yusuf dina tun yana yaro bana taba fadar abu yaja amma yau gashi ya dage,to yakamata kuwa in hakura haka"hajiya tace aranta,"Kiyi hakuri farida zansa anemomiki wata amma idan kinada wanda zai nemo miki shikenan"kamar ta rufe yusuf da duka take ji,wato dai da alamun yau babu cin nasara,me hajiya take nufi?Yau goyanbayan danta take kenan?shikenan yaci nasara ya kori gloria abinda ya dade yana mafarki wato burinshi zai cika?kai hmm,"bakomai Hajiya zansa asamomin din nagode"tace cikin wata murya kasa kasa,kiran yusuf akayi awaya ana nemanshi a wajen aikinsu hakan ne yasashi tafiya saida Hajiya tamishi nasihohi kamar kullum akan zaman lafiya,Tabbas yau Hajiya bata birge farida ba don kuwa tunda sukayi aure duk sanda ta kawo mata zance bin bayanta take amma wai yau tabi bayan danta me take nufi,dazatace tacigaba da hakuri?ba danta bane ta isa dashi saifa abinda tace yakeyi amma yau abin mamaki tafada ya mayar kuma tayi shiru,hmm ita tayi maganin abin dakanta to,ina tasan haka ce zata faru da ta sani ma batazo ba
Bata bar gidan ba sai bayan laasar don tun wuri tayi niyyar tafiya amma ta jinkirta don kar ace haushi taji
Koda ta karasa gida,tadda Gloria tayi a compound din gidan saboda batada key,kuma yusuf bai dawo ba,ita dai tasan gloria dama bazata taba tafiya akaran kanta ba ashe ashe korarta yusuf yayi,"Kai anya kuwa zata iya korar yarinyar nan?"keda aka riga aka gama magana dazu ai ba hanaki akayi ki kawo wata ba,bakomai ta tafi din Allah zai baki wadda tafita"cewar wata zuciyar,"kai yusuf bai isa fa yayi nasara ba,bazan kore tan ba din,ba abinda ya isa yayi"tace tareda bude musu kofa suka shige,babu bata lokaci gloria tashiga kitchen sakamakon yunwar da farida tace mata tanaji
Ba awani dade ba kuwa ta kammala komai farida tazauna ci cikeda jin dadi da nishadi,saida tagama sannan ta dauko computer ta don akwai wasu yan abubuwa dazatayi na aiki ta turawa office dinsu ta Email tunda ta dau hutu
Yusuf bai dawoba sai bayan maghrib saidai me?yana shigowa yasan gloria tashigo gidan,saboda wannan warin nata dayake cewa yanaji yajishi,kafin ya karasa cire takalmi kuwa sai gata ta fito daga daki,"wellcom oga"tace tareda yin kitchen,farida na zaune ta mike kafa a kujera tanata danne dannen computer ta tana shan lemo bata ko kalli inda yake ba,"me yarinyar nan take agidannan?"yace cikin wata murya mai kunshe da tsananin bacin rai da ita kanta faridan batasan yanada ita ba,"me kuwa takeyi banda abinda tasabayi"tace cikeda karfin hali,batreda ta kalleshi ba"nazata dazu angama magana an gama yanke hukunci,ko kuwa tsabar raini ne da rashin kunya irin naki zaisa k
"Dont you dare,ya isheka kuma,kada ka kuskura kace zaka gayamin magana,duk waye yajawo komai?ko don kaga nadawo gidanka kuma nadawo bance maka komai ba shiyasa zaka nemi kagayamin magana,to ba mantawa nayi ba da irin cin mutumcin dakamin,"ta hayyako mishi,"ba wannan zancen nakeyi ba ki gaya mata ta tattara yanata yanata tabar gidan nan tun dare baiyi ba don wallahi na rantse yarinyar nan bazata kwana agidannan ba sai ta tafi,"yace tareda hayewa sama,"au harda wani rantsuwa to kuwa wallahi kai zakayi kaffara,don kuwa babu inda zata",tace tareda cigaba dashan lemonta,zaman ne taga ya gagareta saboda tsabar masifa, dakyar ta tashi cikeda jaraba,tabishi saman,duk abinda akeyi gloria najinsu lekowa tayi taga farida tabar wayarta,hakanne yabata damar dauka ta lalubo num yusuf ta kwafa a tata wayar,"badai korata zaayi ba?Gwara in sami abinda zai dinga debemin kewa ina rage zafi"tace tayi daki,"Tunda farida ta hausaman take balai ta tarar da kofar dakinshi a rufe don yasan haka zata iya faruwa sanin hali,saida yagama duk abinda yake sanan ya fito lokacin harta dawo kasan tazauna tacigaba da huci,tana zaune taga ko kulata baiyi ba ya nufi kofar dakin gloria,yafara knocking gudu kada ya shiga kai tsaye yaganowa kanshi tunda yaga batada nutsuwa,tanaji taki budewa,duk faridan na zaune,ja da baya yayi yazo ya daki kofar ta wangame dama ba irin masu kwarin nan bane cen,saida farida taji tsoro don tasan tabbas ranshi yakai kololuwa wajen baci kenan,"ni saan wasan kine?"yaceda glorian,shiru tayi tayi tsuru tsuru don itama ta tsorata dashi tunda taga ya karya kofa,"ki hada abinda zaki hada naki ki fito ki tafi gidanku i dont want you here"yace da ita,shiru tayi tana nuku nuku,"5mins"ya daka mata tsawa jikinta yafara rawa,babu halin roko,ita kanta faridan yabata tsoro hakan ne ma yasa takasa cewa komai don yadda taganshi yau bata taba ganinshi ba zai iya mata dukan tsiya,"yanzu duk soyayyar nan dakike mishi haka zaki hakura ki tafi ki barshi?"Wata zuciyar tace da gloria,hakan ne yasata tunani harda yan hawayenta kai so baiyi ba wannan shine son maso wani,minti biyar din nacika yashiga dakin duk wani abu nata daya gani yafara yo wurgi dashi,sai kuwa tasa kuka,ko kallonta baiyi ba saida ya tabbata babu komai a dakin sanna yace "wuce muje",ta tsaya gardama "pls na oga plz"ganin yafara ciro belt dinshi ne yasata fita a guje tareda tsitsince yan kayayyakinta,"zuwa tayi tarike kafar farida tana rokonta,akan tasa baki amma ahalin daake ciki ita kanta tasan abubuwan sunfi karfinta babu abinda zata iya,ganin dai dagaske idan ta tsaya yusuf dukanta zaiyi hakan yasa tafita daga gidan aguje,"kada kasake barinta tashigo min gida"yusuf yaceda maigadin nasu,ya juya yayi ciki ya haye sama
"Hajiya kowa fa yasan halin yusuf,wannan abune dani aganina bazai taba aikatawa ba dukda dai kinsan dan Adam yakan chanja,yarinyar nan fa(farida)kamar batada gaskiya,"cewar Aisha bayan Hajiya ta labarta mata komai dake faruwa tsakaninshi da farida,"nima ina wannan tunanin to amma kuma kinsan namiji ne halayyar nan tasu saisu,tason mulki danuna isa,kuma abinda yake bani mamaki shine shifa bai taba zuwa yasameni yace tayi mishi wani abu ba,har bugar cikinshi nake amma sai yace komai kalau,kullum itace mai kawomin kara yamata kaza yamata kaza,kuma gashi sai rama yakeyi,sai nake ganin mutumin da mace take cewa yana kuntata mata take nuna ya isa da gidanshi ne zai dinga irin wannan rama haka?ko bakiga yadda yazama bane?"Nagani wallahi duk wanda yaganshi dole zai gano akwai abinda ke damunshi"cewar Aisha,"to Allah dai ya daidaita yabasu ikon Hakuri da juna"Amin tace

Tabbas rasa abinda ke mata dadi ma tayi,"to wai shin yusuf daina sonta yayi ne kome?don inda dane fa duk abubuwan nan bazai iya mata su ba,amma yau gashi agabanta ya tapka rashin mutumci har yana neman yayi duka,"hmm daga inje gida in dawo shikenan yabi ya birkice,to ma ai ni yakamata ace ina jin haushinshi bayan duk irin abubuwan dayamin,na tafi bai damu ya bini ba ya dawo dani,ko kirana awaya banci daraja yayi ba"haka dai tazauna tanata sake sake a ranta,in takama tayi mitarta afili,kuma taki amincewa dacewar fa itace silar komai ita tajawo ya zama hakan datake cewa yazama tunda ita dai tasan bata laifi kullum akan gaskiyarta take,"nashiga uku"tace tareda zabura,bayan ta tuno rantse rantsen data gamayi akan cewar Gloria bazata bar gidan ba bai isa kuma yayi komai ba to gashi dai anyi koma an gama har abu yazama tarihi,kaffarar datake zance gashi kanta ta hau ita,ya zatayi yanzu itada azumi indai ba na ramadhan ba ko ramuwa bawaniyi take ba saboda yadda take kaunar abinci,tace kuma wahala take, "to ai ba wajibi bane Allah gafururrahim ne zai yafe miki kuma ma ai mai ciki bata azumi"wata zuciyar tace da ita,murmushin jin dadi tayi a fili,tareda cigaba da kallon Tv abinta,taku taji alamun ana saukowa kasan,murtuke fuska tayi ta bata rai,tsakinta data saba tayi sannan tafara kokarin mikewa don tabar wajen "zauna magana nakeso muyi"yace bayan yanemi waje yazauna,"bacci nakeji saika bari saida safe"tacigaba da zura takalmanta,"so nake naja miki kunne dis should be the first and last time dazaki sake zuwa ki hadani da mahaifiyata,wallahi kinji na rantse idan kika kara kuskuren yin hakan duk hukuncin dana yanke ke kika sani,ko kuwa ni dakike zalumta a kullum nataba kai kararki wajen naki iyayen?ko kuma ce miki akayi ni banida zuciya?h
"ina ruwana,wannan kuma kai kaso"ta katseshi cikeda rashin kunya wai ita shahararriya,"yanzu wane kallo kike tunanin hajiya zata dinga miki duk ranar datasan gaskiyar lamura ko kuwa anaki tunanin har abada zakiyi tacin bilis?waike ko tunanin haka ma bakyayi ko kuwa saboda ke kunyarki ma tariga ta kare miki bakida ita?a tsahon rayuwata ban taba gani ko jin labarin mace irinki ba farida tunda na aureki nake bakinciki nake takaici bakuma zan daina fadar hakanba kin cuceni kin yaudareni dakika nunamin ke mutuniyar kirki ce abaya kikazo kika chanja,"kyal kyalewa tayi dawata dariya cikeda rashin mutumci da raini kamar wata tababbiya,"rayuwa ce dai wanda yayi dakyau ma ya ya kare bare wanda yace zaibi son zuc
"kagama?nace kagama?ta hayayyako mishi kallo kawai yabita dashi,"ni banida wannan lokacin dazan tsaya inajin abubuwa marasa amfani bacci nakeji ka tsaidani ni banma san ya akayi natsaya ina jinkaba wallahi"takarasa maganar tana mai yin hanyar kitchen"yarinyar nan batada hankali yusuf ka rabu da ita kawai kadaina biye mata dasannu zata gane kuranta"zuciyarshi tace dashi
"Banason irin tsofaffin nan kinsansu,sai suzo sudinga yiwa mutum iko agida kamar su suka haifeshi,mutum yayi magana ace yace,baka nakeso yarinya yar kauye mummuna"tace(kiran mama tayi awaya don asamo mata mai aiki,dama sammy ce tasan me samowar to yanzu kuwa tasan ko tace tasamo bazata samo ba tunda haushinta takeji)"kin tabbata da amincewar mijinki kike neman mai aikin nan naga cewa kikayi ya kori waccen dakanshi?kinsan banason kidinga abinda mijinki baya goyon bayafa farida nasan gardamarki"mama tace daga daya bangaren,"Wallahi ba karya nakeba mungama magana dashi Allah idan kina fifitashi akaina mama wallahi banajin dadi,yusuf dinnan dakuke gani fa bawai irin mutumin dakuke tunani bane ni kadai nasan halinshi nake kuma hakuri dashi"tace,"banason nadinga jin ira iren zantukan nan daga bakinki fa ,kisani idan kina cutar bawan Allahn nan Allah bazai barki bafa"kamar ya cuta kuma mama?""to cuta mana kina fadar abinda baya aikatawa kina mai kazafi"inji maman,"nifa bana mai karya yadda abubuwan nan suke haka nake fadarsu,sau dayawa inyamin abu saidai inyi shiru kawai bana fada saboda nasan ba lallai ki gasgata ni ba,"Dama haka akeso ai mace takasance mai hakuri dakuma rufawa mijinta asiri bakomai ake fada ba"mama ta bata ansa"Nidai Don Allah asamomin dawuri aikin gidannan yafara isata gashi nagaji"tace don karya bayan babu abinda take bawan nata daya saba komai shi din dai shine"naji,shikenan dai zansa Anemo din amma inada sharadi"(kai itafa shiyasa bataso tasako mama a harkar nan ba saboda tasan halinta kawai don dai babu inda zataje tasamone dakanta kuma tayi hakan ne da biyu ko da yusuf din yace kaza kaza akan yarinyar sai tace ai dai ba ita tasamota ba mama ce"eh inaji"banaso in kawo yarinyar mutane kice zaki dinga musguna mata kamar yadda kuka saba ato suma yaya ne ba fadowa sukayi daga sama ba haifarsu akayi,kuma anasonsu farida banaso inji wani zance mara dadi,idan kika bari wani abu yafaru saina sassaba miki wallahi"na chanja fa ni mai ma zai hadani da ita kawai tayi aikinta shine kawai saimu zauna lafiya amma idan tace zata zakemin to kuwa zan bata mamaki" tace,"au zaki bata manaki?to sai kije ki nemo dakanki mara kunya don kuwa bazai yiwu ba mutane suna ganin mutumcina su yarda dani subani amana kice zaki bada mamaki,sai anjima""wallahi zan kula inshaallah"tace sannan suka dan fara taba hira lokacin take fadawa maman ta dau leave
"Hmm nasan halin yarinyar nan sarai bazai yiwuba inje in samo mata yarinya tacewa mijinta nice na samo duk yazata tunaninmu daya,yamana kudin goro to ni da hankalina sarai"cewar mama don abin bazai mata dadi ba idan mai aikin nan bada amincewar yusuf zaa kawota ba yaji kuma ita takawo ai sai ya zata sai ahankali dai kawai,tana shirin kiranshi saiga nashi kiran yashigo "ah kaga dan halak" tace tareda dauka da sallama,bayan sun gaisa ne sai kuma yayi shiru,"ya ya akayi yusuf?"tace "hm um bakomai dama kira nayi kawai mugaisa"yace,"Allah sarki nima yanzu nake shirin kiranka ai,farida tacemin ka sallami wannan mai aikin meya faru ne?"wallahi Yarinyar ce batada nutsuwa mama,nima banso akayi hakan ba don babu yadda zanyi ne,gani nayi barinta gidan shine mafi alkhairi"yace "to dama tace asamo watane shine nakeso inji idan babu matsala tunda ga yadda akayi da waccen din,"ah eh babu komai inshaallah ni nace ma tasamo wannan din tunda babu dadi na sallami waccen din kuma tazauna babu mai taimakonta"yace"to mashaallah Allah ya daidaita acigaba da hakuri dai ayita hakuri"cewar mama,"bakomai mama inshaallah nagode"yace sukayi sallama
Kiran maman yayi da niyyar sanar da ita halinda ake ciki,dukda kuwa zuciyarshi bata gama aminta da hakan ba,amma bashida wani zabi banda yayi hakan tundadai ita batada niyyar chanjawa,sai kuma daya kira din sai kawai yaji bazai iya ba bai kamata ba,ribar mezai samu don ya hadata da iyayenta?hakan bashida wani alfanu,kuma a yadda yasan mahaifinta ba lallai ya tsawatar mata ba,saima yaga laifin shi watakil,maman ce dama mai kokarin yimusu fada da nasiha,kowa ma yasani,amma yusuf baisan da haka ba sai bayan aurensu dawani lokaci,don a iyaka binciken dasukayi kafin aure basuji komai ba mara dadi gameda faridan ko gidansu,sai daga baya labari yake riskarshi nacewar fa su Yan gatan mahaifinsu ne basa laifi,kuma mahaifinsu zai iya kaiwa kowane mataki idan aka taba mishi yara,kowane hukunci yakama yankeshi yake,shiyasa ma har ya kashewa yarshi aure,shiyasa ma rashin iya girkin farida yadaina damunshi don ance basa aikin komai itada yanuwanta ko mahaifiyarsu tasakasu don su koya Sai Abba yadinga fada,yaranshi bazasu sha wahala ba meye amfanin masu aikin gidan daya tara,shiyasa dukkaninsu babu abindasuka iya,(kunsan zancen duniya baya buya masu karatu)to duk yusuf yasan da abubuwan nan amma ya hadiyesu yake cigaba da hakuri,don ko dayaje gaida Hajiya watarana saida ta tunkareshi da zancen na cewar taji kaza da kaza akan matarshi,atake ya musa yace mata jita jita ne kawai irin na mutane marasa son azauna lafiya,kuma yayi hakan ne don tsananin son faridan dayake dakuma gudun abinda zaije ya dawo,to amma duk irin wannan hakuri dayakeyi Bazaisa farida tayi hankali ba tasan ciwon kanta
Yau kimanin sati daya kenan da faruwar lamarin kememe yusuf ya fita harkar ta yadaina kulata ko da wasa,ita kanta abin yanason yafi karfinta don tunda suke bai taba mata hakan ba,shi kuwa yanayin hakan ne da gangan don yaga kozata shiga hankalinta,amma ina saima kara shahara datake ita adole shi zai sauko ya bata hakuri kar ajinta ya zube,ita take shiga kitchen tayi girkinta,shikuwa sai yayi niyyar girkin yakeyi,don bama ya dawowa gidan sai dare dama don ita yake dagewa yayi girkin,to ya barta ta karata,tunda ya fuskanci nuna mata kula dayakeyi ne dayawa da soyayya yasa take sangarcewa,ko ya dawo yaganta a palo baya kulata saidai yayi sallama kamar yadda yasaba,inta ansa kanta,"wai wannan meyake nufi danine?gaba muke ko me"take tambayar kanta"to ba dole yayi fushi dake ba duk irin abubuwan dakike mishi shima fa mutum ne yanada zuciya,ki yarda kin mishi ba daidai ba kawai kibashi hakuri awuce wajen kinsan halinshi shi ba abokin zafi bane wata zuciyar tace,"tab wato yacigaba da rainani kenan ajina ya zube badani zaayi wanan shashancin ba "tace afili tare dayin kwafa ai indai bazai sauke girman kai ba yabani hakuri saidai mucigaba da zama ahaka,yacigaba da daukan zuga"tace

Mama dakanta taso kawo mata yarinyar,amma hakan bai samu ba sakamakon uzuri datake dashi,dole ta hadota da direbansu na gida,don sai azalzalarta take, faridan,tana mita tana zabga karya wai tagaji abubuwa sun mata yawa ga kwanakin haihuwa na kara matsowa dama kuma mama tace babu zancen zuwa wankan gida saboda batason fitina,Abba kadan yake jira yusuf yadanyi wani abu yace yayi,tunda dama akule yake dashi,ya yanke hukunci wannan yana daya daga dalilan dayasa itama maman tabada azama wajen ganin tasamo mata yarinyar saboda tazauna agidan mijinta,dukda dai haihuwar farice ba yarinya take bukata ba,amma dai idan ta haihun akwai kanwar maman Aunty Rasheeda da mijinta ya rasu tace kada maman taji komai zataje ta zauna da faridan tabata duk wata kulawa data kamata haihuwar fari dole sai ansaka ido

Yadda taga tana shan wahala tana ihu tana kuka ne yasata fashewa da kuka itama don irin mutanen nanne masu saurin kuka dajin tausayi,in banda sannu babu abinda take mata,"mikomin wayata"tace dakyar don tadade da shemewa akasa,tsabar azaba,shi tasake kira da niyyar idan bai dauka ba ko yacigaba da raina mata hankali ta kira mama,don taga wannan ba ciwo bane dazata iya jureshi,ringing daya kuwa ya dauka"yanzunnan zan taho,wai ni yau juliet kika zama ne?Lallai kin dau chaji h

Baiwani dade a hanya ba ya karaso don babu holdup,koda yazo halinda yaganta ciki ne yasa zuciyarshi karaya,tabbas haihuwarce gashi taji jiki,ga abu a gefe ba abinda take sai kuka tana mata sannu,daukota yayi yasata amota sai asibiti
"Allah ya sauketa lafiya dai wannan haihuwa da wahala Allah yakawo dasauki"cewar Abu daaka bari jiran gida,duk ta kasa tsaye takasa zaune

RUWAN DAFA KAI 1 - RUWAN DAFA KAI - Page 2 - Wattpad
RUWAN DAFA KAI 61~65Na SUMAYYA DANZABUWA
Tabbas Farida tasha wahala matuka,don ta dade tana labour har an fara tunanin ko zaa mata cs Allah ya taimaka ta haifo dan kyakkyawan yaro,bandai san wa yayo ba acikinsu tukunna domin kuwa dai indai kyau ne daga ita har yusuf din babu baya
Yusuf kuwa yana waje an hanashi shiga,hankalinshi ya kai koluluwa wajen tashi inbanda adduoi babu abinda ya dukufa dayi ganin anshafe awowi kusan nawa ana abu daya lallai abinnan (haihuwar)ya shallake hankalinshi ya zarce tunaninshi shi dayayi zaton ana shiga da ita zaa cemishi ta haihu amma gashi awanni kusan nawa shiru?,gashi yama kasa sanarda kowa,da yayi tunanin kiran mama ko hajiya sai kuma ya tuna halinda zasu shiga don yasan duk macenda  taji labarin yaruwarta tana labour wani hali take  shiga na rashin kwanciyar hankali,yana cikin wannan yanayin  ne likitan tazo mishi da albishir na cewar farida tasauka lafiya an samu namiji,sujjada ya farayi,cikeda godiyar Allah,murnar dayayi a lokacin  nan bazata fadu ba don abinda ya dade yana fatane yasamu Allah ya rabasu lafiya(Farida da dan),babu wani bata lokaci akace zai iya shiga ganinsu,kasancewar dukanninsu nacikin koshin lafiya
Saida yashiga yagansun tukun hankalinshi ya kara kwanciya,sannan yasamu damar kiransu  Hajiya dasu mama da bash ya sanar dasu labarin mai dadi,kafin kuce meye wannan kowa yafara garzayowa
Gida mama tace ya koma don kwaso  musu kaya dukda dai bawani zama zasuyi ba tunda Allah yasa lafiya ta haihu saidai dan abinda baa rasa ba
ko daya karasa ya shiga palon,da Abu yafara cin karo rikeda qurani alamun ta dade tana karatu,tunda ga abin sallah cen ma ya hango,(bai san tunda suka fita take abu aya ba ga dukufa datayi tanata adduoi duk dan akan farida ta haihu lafiya don yadda taganta dazun nan ta tsorata dayawa),"Ya Auntyn"ta tambaya cikeda damuwa,bayan ta ansa sallamar tashi,ganin murmushin da yusuf yasaki ne yasa zuciyarta dan nutsuwa "tana nan kalau ansamu da namiji"kawai yace, tareda karasawa saman cikin dan sassarfa,"Alhamdulillah Allah nagode maka"tace tareda ci gaba dajin dadi don Allahn dayayi ta tana masifar son yara,shikenan yanzu kullum tasan zata kasance tareda yaron nan,tunda tasan duka ragamar kula dashi hannunta zata dawo yadda ta fuskanci uwar dakin nata batason aiki ko da wasa,wayyo dadi,ko don yaron nan zata ma daina tunanin tafiya don tasan zai dinga debe mata kewa,jikinta ne yayi sanyi kuma,tunowa da halin uwardakin nata,kar tazo kuma tace batasan zance ba ma'ana tace babu mai taba mata da,don zata aikata
Koda yusuf ya karasa dakin farida don kwaso kaya rasa ta inda zai fara ma yayi don kuwa babu abinda ta hada,babu wani shiri,bayan babu yadda baiyi da ita ba akan ta hada kayanta yadda kowace mace take hadawa idan haihuwa ta kusa saboda gudun mantuwa dasauransu, mama ma saida ta tambayeta rannan ko ta hada tace zadai ta hada ashe kuwa bata hada dinba,wayanda idanunshi suka hango su kawai ya dauko itama ya zabo mata
Abu na cikin yan tunane tunanenta Taga yusuf yasake saukowa da yar jaka wannan karon ma fuskarshi cikeda jin dadi da faraa,yazo ya wuceta ya fice kamar ta tambayeshi yaushe zasu dawo,ko ta roki atafi da ita tagano yaron,don ta kagu,amma kafin tagama shawara da zuciyarta har maganar ta fito ya fice,"lallai mutumin nan yanaji da matarshi,ji yadda ya dauketan nan dazu duk yabi ya rikice,oh ni Allah sarki taji dadi tayi saar miji,"tace afili tareda shiga harkarta don soyayyarshi ga matarshi ai ba abinda ya shafeta bane
Saida Farida ta kwana a asibitin sannansuka yo gida da hantsi duk tawani bi ta nutsu kamar ba ita ba (taji ajikinta),don batayi ma tunanin zata kawo iyanzu ba
Tun a Asibitin Aunty Rasheeda tazo don haka tare suka dawo gidan babu bata lokaci kuw tafara bata duk wata kulawa  data kamata itada jaririn,Don Abu saida tazama yar kallo ma saidai abinda baa rasa ba don Aunty Rasheedan  irin matan nanne masu hidima dason aiki,irin marasa son jikin nan,lura da Son yin harkar jaririn da Abu takeyi ne yasa  Aunty Rasheedan  take bata rikonshi lokaci  lokaci gudun masifa irinta farida,to kuma abin mamaki sai taga akan yaron dai faridan  bata wani daga hankali don Abun ta daukeshi,hasalima  indai ba nono zata bashi ba bata fiya daukanshi ba tunda kullum yana wajen Auntyn
Su mama dakowa har yusuf din anso ayi gagarumin taron suna Farida tace bataso,don tunda ta haihun take nuna wasu halaye na daban da da batadasu,kamar yadda take nuna halin ko in kula ga yaron,da kuka datake yawanyi,babu yadda baayi ba ta dage dole suka hakura
Ranar suna aka sawa yaro Muhammadul Amin, sunan Abban faridan,tabbas kowa yayi farinciki da hakan,don dama Hajiya tasan yusuf dai bazai sakawa danshi sunan nashi mahaifin   ba,Itama faridan taji dadi kwarai don bata taba  zata ba,shima Abban dayaji saida yaji kunya,jikinshi kuma yayi sanyi don gashi dai yusuf din dayake yiwa kallon mara nutsuwa mara kunya mara mutumci yabashi mamaki wannan abinne ma yasa yarage jin haushin yusuf din dayake amma har yanzu yana kule dashi saboda duka da zagi da farida tace yana mata
Wannan chanji na farida yafara damunsu kuma musamman ma yusuf,dole yasa Aunty Rasheeda tamata magana akan suje suga likita don shi har yayi yagaji,tace babu inda zata lafiyarta kalau kawai yanaso ya fara raina mata hankaline yadda yasaba,itama Auntyn Abin  yaso yafi karfinta don itama tayi harta gaji faridan tace babu fa inda zataje mai sukeso su maidata ita lafiyarta kalau,hakance tasa Yusuf kiran likitar tazo gida don shidai yasan yadda take abubuwan nan ba lafiyarta kalau ba,"Ba wani abin daga hankali bane "Baby Blues" ne(postpartum depression)mata dayawa suna kamuwa da irin hakan bayan haihuwa amma na dan lokaci ne,kuyi kokari dai kawai kudan dinga yin nesa da yaron daga gareta karta mishi wani abin,sai kuma idan zata shayar dashi a tabbata akwai mai saka mata ido,"cewar likitan"nidai nasan dama abinnan ba haka kawai ba,ko magana fa bata fiya yi ba wanda hakan kuwa ba halinta bane,amma dai zaa kiyaye inshaallah zata iya kaiwa kamar yaushe kenan kafin ta dawo daidai?"yusuf yasake tambaya cikeda kaguwa da damuwa,"karka wani tada hankalinka na dan lokacine ahankali zata daina,babu wani abu inshallah"to shikenan nagode yace sukayi sallama
Ko sati biyun baa cika ba kamar yadda likitar tagayawa yusuf farida tafara nuna halayenta na da,don ita kanta Auntyn saida tayi mamaki "wato yarinyar nan ashe aure bai nutsar da ita ba tana nan da wayannan mugayen bakaken halayen nata kenan na rashin kunya?"wannan dalilin shine yasata tun farko tazo tazauna da ita din don idan ba ita ba babu wanda zai iya zaman sanin halinsu(faridan da sauran yanuwanta)dakowa yayi,to amma me?ita Auntyn tayi tunanin ko tunda tayi aure yakamata ace ta chanja amma ashe babu wani chnaji saima iskancinta daya karu,babu abinda yafi daurewa Auntyn kai kamar yadda taga faridan ta raina mijinta,shikuma yana lallabta,don iyaka zaman datayi dasu ko sau daya bataga yayiwa matar tashi kallon banza ba bare yace zai mayar mata da martani,ko ya auki mataki,duba da irin kalamai marasa dadi datake gaya mishi
Ganin wannan abu ba mai karewa bane yasa Auntyn zaunar da yusuf din don ta tabbatar da abinda take tunani,"yusuf wai meyake faruwa ne"a ina?me kika gani Aunty"yace cikeda ladabi,don babu abinda yake kara  birgeta dashi sama da irin biyayyar shi bayan kyautatawa,shikuwa yanayin hakan ne saboda a ganinshi bakowa bane zai iya zuwa yazauna da matarka yadinga kula da ita da danka kyauta,duk wanda zai maka haka kuwa yamaka komai kuma ya cancanci ka kyautata mishi,"matarka farida,meke faruwa ne ko har yanzu bata warke din bane?"Cewar Auntyn,yar dariya kawai yayi,"lafiyarta kalau Aunty Haka take ai"kawai yace,duba datayi da idan ta matsa da tambaya babu abinda zai fada mata hakan ne yasata hakura,da tambayar,"ka kara hakuri yusuf nasan kanayi amma dai ka kara kaji nayi tunanin ko ta chanja ashe har yanzu hakan take"tace,sannan tacigaba dayimishi yan nasihohi masu kwantar da hankali,"wato dai albasa batayi halin ruwa ba duk yanuwan mahaifiyar farida da ita kanta mahaifiyartata dukkansu babu masu irin hali nata duk sunada kirki a iyaka saninshi,kenan dai mahaifin nasu ne silar  zamar dasu hakan kenan?lamari yana kara gasgatuwa,Allah ya kyauta
Cen kuma Bash ne da matarshi Amina suke fafatawa don tace bazatazo barka ba,tayiwa farida na Allah da Annabi kuma,tunda suke basu taba kace nace ba shida ita sai wannan karon,"matar nan tanuna batasona karara kaima wayasan me take cewa akanka?dolene sai nayi harka da ita?ai ba yusuf kadai bane mai mata cikin abokannanka ko kaga ina yiwa sauran haka?kabarni kawai basai naje ba kai tunda kaje ai shikenan Allah ya raya yaro"yanzu akan matsalar wasu kika fusata haka har kike neman kimin rashin kunya Amina?"Ba rashin kunya nakeso namaka ba kafi kowa sanin halina tunda muke dakai ka taba jan layi na tsallaka?to mezai hana wannan karon tunda kaga na dage ka hakura kawai ka barni?ni so nake kawai ka fuskanci gaskiyar lamarin nan,abinnan fa guda dayand  farida bata sona bakuma taso  tayi harka dani to don me zan dinga nace mata,?nasan yusuf amininka ne tare naganku kadamj dashi to
"kufa mata matsalarku kenan daukaka zance,yanzu meya na girmama zancen nan haka?"ya katseta"nasha gayamiki kidaina biyewa  abubuwa irin waynannan ke fa mai hankalice da nutsuwa Amina,babu kyau kace wai duk abinda aka maka saika rama meye aciki don kinje ai ba don ita zaki ba sai don yaron dakuma babanshi haba Aminata"yace cikin kwantar da murya bata musu da mijinta amma gashi akan farida sunayi gaskiya taji rashin  son matar nan ya karu aranta,gashi ta dalilinta tana neman tabata ran mijinta,"zanje amma wannan ne karo na karshe"bakomai kishirya ina jiranki"yace
Yan wajen aikinsu farida ma duk sun zazzo,harda sammy,don ba irin mutanen nan bane masu riko,an riga an wuce wajen amanta dakomai,rayuwar kenan
Kasa shiru Da irin abubuwan dake faruwa agidan Aunty tayi,abubuwa ne kamar a film,yusuf din kamar tsoron faridan yake,sai abinda tace zaiyi yana gudun bata mata rai,lallai dole tazauna da faridan  don jin dalilinta na raina miji datayi,"nifa ba rainashi nayi ba kawai  dai ina kwatarwa kaina yanci ne da mutumci kinsan mazan nan na yanzu  idan sukaga ka fiya musu biyayya sai su rainaka"tace cikeda rashin mutumci,"ke ni kike gayawa haka?"Cewar Aunty a fusace don dama faridan ta kwana biyu tana bata mata rai takuma lura da tsantsan rainin datake nuna mata sharewa kawai take,don tanayin komai ne saboda yaruwarta,dakuma yusuf din,"to meye aciki menace?yanzu fa sai kice rashin kunya namiki ko?"tasake cewa,tareda cigaba da taunar chewing gum dinta,"lallai farida wato baki chanja ba,ni kike gayawa wannan maganar,to kuwa kibi ahankali miji kike wulakantawa ba saurayi ba,ni nazata ko kyautata mikin da yakeyi yaci ace yaci darajar hakan,tunda nazo gidannan yaron nan yake fadi tashi dake,h
"da yaushe kikazo gidan dahar zaki bada shaidarshi?mijinki ne ko mijina?"tasake hayayyakowa, wannan karon harda daga murya,"too,har kik kai nan?lallai zaki iya nada min duka kenan?wato ni kike gayawa haka saboda bakida mutumci?wannan rashin tarbiyyar dai kinsan daga inda kika gadoshi, don yaruwata da danginmu baki daya bahaka muke ba,mara kunya fitsarrarriya,"To agaskiya nagaji da irin bakaken  maganganun dakike fadamin agidannan kullum,kina zagina ni ina ganin gwara kawai ki tafi,don bzai yiwu ba kice zakizo har cikin gidana k
wani wawan mari Auntyn ta tsinketa dashi wanda yasata gigicewa,tunda ta sakankance bata zata ba,kasa kuka ma tayi tsananin gigicewa,don tunda take ma ita baa taba marinta ba,,"kinyi kadan wallahi,kuma dai kinsan  ai ko kince ko bakice ba dama nagama zaman gidan nan yau tunda ke bakisan mutumci nikuma da abin kirki bai karbeni ba,ai na dade da lura da take takenki kyaleki kawai nake kuma wallahi kikace zaki sake fadar wata magana anan ta rashin tarbiyya saina miki shegen duka, bawai kina ganin kina iskanci kina cin bulus ba,sai Allah yasakawa bawan Allah,shashasha kawai"cewar Auntyn tareda tashi tashige tahado  kayanta,don taga idan takara wani dan lokaci agidan zata iya yiwa farida dukan tsiya,Kuka Abu tasaka ganin dai dagaske Auntyn tafiya zatayi dukda dai batasan meya faru ba amma ta lura kamar ranta a abace  yake don tunda tazo gidan inbanda mutumci da girmamawa babu abinda yake shiga tsakaninsu,bayadda  ta iya dole sukayi sallama ta jaddadmata kara hakuri da uwar dakin nata
