RUWAN DAFA KAI 66~70Na SUMAYYA DANZABUWA
Waya ta dauka ta kira mama,da maman har bazata dauka ba don Auntyn takirata ta labarta mata komai,inda maman tadinga bata hakuri takuma ji babu dadi,don farida bata kyauta mata ba,babu tantama dole tanuna mata bacin ranta tunda batada mutumci,daukan wayar tata maman tayi don taga sai kiranta take,kuma bata raba dayan biyu,zata kawo mata kara ne akan abinda yafaru tsakaninta da Auntyn,daukan wayar keda wuya,tajita ta fashe dawani matsanancin kuka"Lafiya dai ko?maman tace,amma babu abinda take sai kuka,"kin kirani kinamin kuka na tambayeki dalili kinmin shiru zan fa kashe wayata!"maman tace,ganin maganar ba ta waya bace, yasa ta kashe wayar,tadauki key din motarta harta kai kofar dakin tadawo,tasakawa Amin din Pillow,gefe da gefe,sakamakon bacci dayakeyi tayi tafiyarta
Ko data karasa gidan ma kukan ta na iskanci tacigaba kamar yadda tasaba duk sanda takawo kara tana jira taji maman tafara lallabata tana rarrashinta don tafadi abinda ke faruwa,jira take jira take amma shiru,ganin maman na kallon Tv cikeda nishadi ne yasata sake fashewa da kuka wai dole sai maman tanuna damuwarta ta tambayeta,ko kallonta batayi ba saima remote data dauka ta karo volume,jikinta ne yafara sanyi to ko dai Auntyn tafadawa maman?don yadda ta nuna rashin damuwarta kamar taji?to ko taji ai nima inada nawa bangaren na labarin" tace azuciyarta,itama maman jira kawai take taji irin sharrin dazata harhada,don sanaarta ce,sanin hali ai kuwa babu wani bata lokaci tafara shirgawa maman karairayi iri iri tayi kare karenta tayiyyi sharri kamar yadda tasaba,da abinda yafaru da wanda bai faru ba duk saida ta hada,"da wannan dalilin ne yasaki baro gidan mijin naki ko tambaya babu ko kuwa kin tambayeshi?kuma ina dan naki?"mama ta titsiyeta cikin bacin rai,"baya nan(mijin nata), shikuma(dan)bacci yake"sai kuma kikayo gaban kanki kika kamo hanya ko?ke kuma wato haka kike?kina girma kina cin kasa?wannan wane irin hauka ne iye?ya zaayi ki kamo hanya ki fito ki baro dan dakika haifa yaro dan jariri,wai don yana bacci,?a ina kiga uwa tanayin haka?,lallai babu tantama na tabbatar bakida hankali to,yanzu dakikzo kina gayamin wannan shirmen mezanyi akai?ko kuwa an gayamiki kowa irin kine?yau da bansan halinki ba sai kice zaki fadamin abu in yarda amma nariga na dade dasanin ke kin kai kololuwa wajen hada karya da chanja zance"nif
"zaki tashi ki bacemin dagani ko saina kara miki?"maman ta hayyako mata,baki bude ta tsaya kallon maman"au yanzu duk abinda nagaya miki bazakice komai bama, kina nufin itace akan daidai,?kina gani fa har cikin gidana tazo tamin dukan tsiya amma kice in tashi in tafi,nice ma nayi ba daidai ba wato kawai don yaruwar kice?wai meyasa bakyasona m
"ai bata karasa ba Maman ta kara kwasheta da mari har sau biyu,tasaki wata kara kuwa don sun shigeta,"tun kafin ki sanar dani karairayinki tafadamin komai shashasha dama jiran ki nake don nasan zaayi haka,farida bakiji dadin haliba wallahi,ko arzikina bata ci ba ki raga mata,to ko dayake ni dinma meye tunda inda kina ganin mutumcina ai bazaki mata abinda kikayi ba,sakarya kawai,tunda haka kika zaba saiki cigaba ki kara kaimi don Allah kar ki daina abinda kike,nidai Allah yasani ina bakin kokarina akanku amma tunda komai nayi ban iya ba kunfini iyawa,shikenan duniya cedai gaku gata wanda baizo bama jiranshi take"cewar mama cikin fada,kus tayi agefe sai aikin hawaye"kuma ki tashi kibarmin gida tunda har kina tinkaho kema kinada gidan miji kinayin gori, nima nan gidan mijina ne,"tsayawa tayi tana nuku nuku,"zaki tashi ko kuwa saina sassaba miki?"maman ta daka mata tsawa, cikeda bacin rai,wanda faridan ita kanta tsahon rayuwarta bata taba ganinta ahaka ba,cikin sauri sauri tafito don yadda ran mama yabaci zata iya komai,kama hanya tayi tayi gida,tana tafe tana kuka,gashi Abba baya gari dama shi taso tagayawa tasan shine mai rarrashinta ya share mata hawaye yabi bayanta,In ta kama ya bi mata hakki,amma banda mama tadinga abu kamar ba ita ta haifesu ba,kuma tasan tayi hakan ne don kawai Auntyn yaruwarta ce
Tana fita bata dade ba yusuf yadawo,tunda yashigo yake jiyo kukan Amin,"meya sami yaron nan ne"yace afili tareda karasawa saman dasauri don baya kaunar jin kukan dan nashi ko da wasa,ko da ya karasa ganin yaron yayi gashi shikadai akan gadon, har ya gangaro yazo bakin gado saura kadan ya fado,kasancewar yafara wayo yayi yan watanni,"subhanallahi"cewar yusuf din tareda yarda jakar kayan dake hannunshi,wasu laces ne da atmapopi yasiyowa Auntyn,don kusan kullum cikin siyo mata abubuwa yake duk don murnan kula da su farida datakeyi hakan yana mai dadi,karasawa yayi yadau yaron dasauri,"ina farida tashiga tabar yaron nanne shi kadai?"yace bayan ya bude bathroom din bai ganta ba,saida yaduba ko ina asaman nan babu ita,babu Aunty,sannan ya sauko yafara kwalawa Abu kira,tunda ita ba kamar gloria ba yana dan kulata har yasakata ma abubuwa wani lokacin,"zainab"yacigaba dakiranta itama shiru,yaje yana knocking dakinta shiru,ita kuma tun dazu da ta tafi raka Aunty ta wuce islamiyya abinta
Ran yusuf ne yakai koluwar bacci,wannan wane irin abune,dazasu fita dukansu subar yaro shikadai,wane irin ma haukane,jin maigadi na kiciniyar bude gate ne yasashi lekawa ta window,ganin farida tashigo ne yasashi ma sandarewa yakasa motsi don abin yafi karfin ayi mamaki,"lallai ma farida fita tayi kenan wato tabar mishi yaro shi kadai agida,har zai fado daga gado kamar ba ita tahaifeshi ba to ko wahalar datasha wajen haihuwa ai yaci ace tana daraja shi,yau ko ba ita ta haifeshi ba kyautarshi aka bata baici ace tayi haka ba,baigama tunanin ba tashigo palon cikeda sake saken irin hukuncin dazata dauka akan Auntyn don bazata mareta ba taci bulus ita ba yarinya ba bakomai ba,saita gane kurenta,"ina kikaje?"ya watso mata tambayar don bata ma kula dashi ba,"gida"tabashi ansa a takaice,tana shirin wucewa,"gida?"ya maimaita tareda jinjina zancen,"ke kadai kika je gidan ko tareda Auntyn kuka tafi naga itama bata nan"yasake cewa,"ta tafi dazu"tace atakaice irin tagaji dabashi ansar nan tanufi hanyar sama,"dakata ai bangama ba"tsayawa tayi a inda take don tasan batada gaskiya kuma abubuwan dasuke damunta yau sunada yawa,"shine kuma don rashin sanin ciwon kai zaki fita kibar danki agida?who does that?"gashi kuwa nayi,gidan namu karshen duniya ne da don na dan je nadawo zaayita yaya tawa,kuma dolene duk inda zani saina tafi da yaro?naga bacci yake lokacin kuma nasa mai pillow,yanxu daban tafi dashi dinba mai yasam
"you are very stupid"yadaka mata tsawa,"ni ka zaga?"ta katseshi,"zan miki abinda yafi wannan ma,wai ke wace irin macece?ya Allah wannan wace irin macece?wallahi ban taba ganin mace irinki ba farida,nazata duk rashin mutumcin dazakiyi aduniyar nan akaina zai kare to ashe nayi kuskure,danki ma,dan dakika haifa dan cikinki daya tsaga jikinki ya fito bai tsira ba farida waye zai tsira awajenki idan zaki yiwa danki haka?wai wannan wane irin hauka ne?"yace cikin fada,wanda hakan yayi daidai da dawowar Abu daga isamiyya,da sallamarta tashigo taga ana fada,simi simi tayi hanyar daki,"ke kuma ina kikaje?"itama yusuf din ya watso mata tambayar,"naam,ni?"aa ni"nace ina kikaje daga ina kike"ya daka mata tsawa,tafara karkarwa,ranshi ya baci yama manta tana zuwa makaranta,"daga makaranta nake walla
"shiga ciki"ya ktseta,don bayaso taji ko taga yanayiwa faridan haka dukda kuwa ita(faridan)ba damuwarta bane agaban kowa ma yi mai take,"walahi inda wani abu yasami yaron nan bazan taba yafe miki ba,"yace cikin sassauta murya tareda kama hanyarshi ya fita,da yaron a kafada
Kasa cewa komai tayi saboda yau bakin cikin datake ciki yamata yawa,ga na Aunty,ga na Mama,ga nashi shima to wai dame zataji ne

2
Yusuf nashirin fita daga gidan,har ya shige mota da yaron yaga an bude gate,ya hango su Hajiya,da yayyensshi guda biyu,kuma da gidan Hajiyan yayi niyyar zuwa,fitowa yayi daga motar tareda dan wayancewa wai don karsu fahimci wani abu"aa kune bako sanarwa?"yace cikeda farinciki,"Hajiya kinga abinda nake gaya miki ko?basabanba"cewar Aisha,(wai don anga yafito da yaron daga cikin mota ance kullum yana tareda yaron)"to meye aciki shida danshi karku takurawa yarona fa"Hajiyan tace,cikin wasa da dariya,"atoh dai gwara kusani"yace tareda musu iso cikin gidan
Neman waje sukayi suka zauna harda shi,ganin an shafe kusan minti nawa ahaka ne yasa Hajiya tambayar wai faridan bata nan ne?"tana nan inaga dai bacci take dayake bata danjin dadine"yace,"wayyo,Allah sarki aida ka duba tadan sauko angaisa tunda su asmau komawa zasuyi sai kuma an kara ganinsu"cewar Hajiyan,"to bari inje"yace ya tashi ya hau saman,bawai don yasan zata sauko ba sai don kawai bin umarnin Hajiya,suna cikin jiran ne Abu ta fito,har kasa ta gaidasu cikeda ladabi,sannan tashiga kitchen don kawo musu ruwa
Ko daya hau saman kin karasawa dakin nata yayi don yasan kawai bata mishi rai zatayi,baikuma san karyar dazai hada musu ba idan bai mata maganar ba,don yasan su masu cewa ne zasu shiga har daki suganta ba ruwansu ganin an zama daya ai,lekawa dakin yayi da niyyar idan yafada mata tanemi tamishi rashin kunya shima ya gaggaya mata magana tunda batada mutumci,saidai kuma me sautin kuka yajiyo yana tashi,mamakine ya isheshi"wai maganar daya matace dazu tasata kukan ko me?to ko dai shiryuwa tafarayi taga abinda ta aikata bata kyautaba?ya tambayi kanshi"amma faridan ce tazama haka?amata magana tazo tana kuka bata maida martani ba dama kuma dazun yayi mamakin shirun datayi ai da walakin kuma tace mishi Aunty ta tafi anya kuwa?anya?"Su Hajiya ne sukazo ki sauko ku gaisa"yabata rai,banza tayi dashi"idan baki sauko ba raina zai baci farida"yasake cewa,"ganin ta tashine hawaye duk shabe shabe a fuska yasashi dan jin dadi,"ikon Allah wato tabbas maganata ta ratsata gashi tafara shiryuwa ta ji ni"yace aranshi cikeda jin dadi,bathroom yaga ta shige alamun zata wanko fuska kenan"saidai kuma me kusan minti goma shiru taki fitowa yana tsaye yana jira, kodayaje ya murda kofar ji yayi ta rufo taciki ashe,"zaki bude kofar nan ko kuwa,idan kika bari nashigo bazakiji da dadi ba"yace tareda bubbuga kofar,ganindai ba budewa zatayi ba kuma yana bata lokaci ne yasa yasaita kanshi ya sake saukowa,"ai wato tanajin jiki fa,"yace tun kafin a tambayeshi"jikin nan nata zafi rau kamar kamar me,bazata iya saukowa ba,"yasake cewa tareda kin hada ido dasu don yasan zasu iya gano karya yake,"to ba sai mu h
"aa bacci take dama dakyar tasamu tasamu baccin ma dazun,zatazo muku ai inshaallah tanajin jiki kwarai da gaske"cewarshi tareda sako wasu zantukan don a basar da zancen,"naji kuma kamar ana buga kofa dazu daka hau?"cewar yaya Asmau,tsuru tsuru yayi,yayi saurin kirkiro karya,"kofar dakince take dan chijewa shiyasa sai an dan bubbugata tukun"yace
Suna shirin tafiya ne Sukaga Abu tafara kawo abinci,ashe duk kamshin dasuke ji daga kitchen dinne girkinta ne,"aa to ke kuma haka akeyi dama girki kike tayi to ai mu tafiya ma zamuyi"cewar Hajiya,yar dariya tayi kawai don Abu akwai kunya,saida tagama hada musu komai tashige daki,bubbudawa sukayi,suka dinga mamaki dukkaninsu domin kuwa basu zata ba wannan yar yarinyar ce ta iya hanzari haka harta gama wanann girkin cikin kankanin lokaci?,lallai tayi kokari takuma basu mamaki,su Asmau ne suka zuzzuba a tray babbba don sun sabacin abinci ahaka dukkaninsu a kwano daya,ganin yusuf yaja baya ne yasa su maida dubansu gareshi,"meye hakan"Aisha tace,"na koshi"yace tareda cigaba dayiwa Amin wasa,"kullum ne kake samun damar cin abinci da yanuwanka?,maza ka sauko kasa albarka"Hajiya ta matsa mishi,shi ba abin yace baya cin abincin mai aiki ba yanzu hajiya ta fusata dashi,tace bai manta da wancen lamarin ba,Abun ya kara kwalawa kira tazo yabata Amin din tarikeshi sugama cin abinci don yarinyar a nutse take komai
Lomar daya kai ta farko ita tasashi shiga wani hali,don saida ya sosa kunne,"kai!"yace aranshi tareda dan dakatawa,har suna tambayarshi ko lafiya,"bakomai fa abu na tuno"yace suka cigaba daci ana hira,"wannan yarinya dai akwai kokari ji girki kamar ba ita tayi ba"suka dinga cewa dukda dai har yau basu tabacin girkin matar gidan ba,(farida),shima yayi mamaki matuka don bai taba zata iya girkin nata da farida take fada yakai haka ba yadaiyi tunanin kawai don dai ita kwadayayyaiyace shiyasa komai yake mata dadi,ashe dai ashe dai
Haka suka gama cin abincin cikeda nishadi abin gwanin ban shaawa sannan suka tashi suka tafi,saida yadawo daga rakasu abu ta dawo mishi da yaron sannan ta gyara wajen
Zamanshi yayi a kasan don bamashi da lokacin dazaije yana tambayarta(farida)dalilin kukanta tama zo ta bata mishi rai abanza yadda tasaba,tunda ita baa mata gwaninta,idan taga dama tazo tafada dakanta yace aranshi,karar shigowar sako wayarshi yaji ya dauko yaduba,number rannan yagani babu suna,an ciko shafika da kalaman soyayya,kamar dai na kwanaki,hakan ne yasashi jan tsaki ya wurgar da wayar gefe

"Hajiya kamar fa akwai abinda yake faruwa agidnnan?yusuf dai bayason fada ne kawai"cewar Asmau bayan sun kama hanya?"wane gidan?"Hajiya tace cikeda rashin fahimtar zancen don sun biya gidan wani  kawunta dasuka baro gidansu yusuf din,"Haba ashe dai ba ni kadai na lura ba,yusuf fa akwai abinda yake boyewa yaron nan,kullum naganshi a firgice yake duk yabi ya ufita hayyaci,tunda yayi aure duk yabi ya chanja kamanni ana ganinshi ansan yana cikin damuwa amma yayita musawa"Aisha ta kara, "Au sai yanzu nagano inda zancen naku ya dosa ai,Amma meyasa kuka ce haka?"hajiya ta katsesu,"Nifa inaga matar nan tashice take gana mishi azaba Hajiya,don idan kika lura dashi zaki gane baa nutse yake ba"hmmm da gaskiyarku to amma ya zanyi dashi na tambaya na tambaya yacemin babu komai komai lafiya,saima matarshi datake yawan kawomin kararshi,akai akai kwana biyu dai banganta ba bansani ba ko lamuran haihuwar ne suka sha mata kai,"ta kara,"kunsan Halin yusuf da hakuri da kau dakai,ga dauriya tun yana dan karaminshi ba mutum bane dazaizo yace muku ana mai badaidai ba ko wane da wance sun mai kaza,mutumin dayake ansa laifikan wasu bayan bashi ya aikata ba wai don azauna lafiya ko kun manta?banda na saitashi ai da tuni ya dade da tsunduma kanshi cikin matsala,ban fiya damun kaina bane da lamarinshi da matarshi saboda nasan halin maza,zai iya yiwuwa abinda take fadamin din gaskiya ne tunda dan adam ne shi,zai iya chanjawa akoda yaushe,amma koma dai menene Allah ya kawo sauki yakuma bayyana gaskiya"Amin sukace dukansu suka cigaba da yan hirarrakinsu

kasa nutsuwa yayi yanata fatan dai Allah yasa ba abinda yake tunani bane aranshi na cewar farida tamata hali(saboda yadda yaga faridan dazu yasha jinin jikinshi)wayarshi ya dauko yafara lalubar lambar Auntyn amma shiru,bama ta shiga,shidai yanata fatan Allah yasa lafiya gashi dare yanayi kuma ko gidanta baisani ba don basu taba zuwa ba dama iyakarsu da ita waya
Haka rayuwa tacigaba da kasancewa agidan kullum yusuf dai yanata hakuri farida tana cigaba da iskanci,saukin daaka samu ma shine Amin din yafison madara nonon bai dameshi ba,kuma itama hakan yamata dadi don dama tadade da yanke hukunci idan ta haihu wata shida zata shayar kawai don bazai yiwuwa nononta yazama kamar slippers,da iliminta dakomai tazama jagwal,hakan ne yasa  idan tanajin haushi shiga daki take ta kullo kanta batareda ta muna damuwarta ga yaron ba nako yana jin yunwa ko bayaji saboda tasan zaisha madara,dama zancen wankanshi da duk wani abu nashi Abu ce,saidai dan abinda baa rasa ba don kusan rabin kayan shi ma suna dakin Abun,tunda ita  take wankesu,ita take mishi komai yusuf yana matukar jin takaicin hakan,don ya tsani yaga uwa nanuwa dan data haifa rashin kulawa,lamarin farida kuwa har yau yakasa gane mata yau zata nuna babu abinda takeso sama da danta gobe ta nuna bata damu dashi ba,ga yaro kullum wayo yake karayi
Ba yadda yusuf baiyi ba akan farida tagaya mishi abinda yafaru Aunty ta tafi kememe taki fada daya matsa sai cewa tayi rufeta tayi da duka haka kawai,"duka kuma ita Auntyn dakanta?"ya nanata,tareda jinjina zancen"ita din fa to meye na mamakin kai fa don bakasan halin matar nan bane shiyasa har kake wano damuwa da ita,ai ba abanza kaga naki sakin jiki da ita ba tun farko ai saboda gudun irin haka ne tunda ni nasan hali,duk hakurin danayi da ita,duk juriyar danayi,kuwa ashe saita bani mamaki" tace,"to amma meya hadaku da har zaa kai ga duka,ni shine abinda bangane ba"meye kuwa ya hadamu ni nama manta meya faru,kasanta dai da nuna isa dason mulki,"ita Auntyn yaushe?ban taba lura ba ni"ya katseta "bazaka lura ba dama,kaga ni bama nason mudinga maganar nan abinda yafaru yariga ya faru kawai amanta a wuce wajen"tace tareda tashi tabar palon"hmm wanda baisan farida ba wallahi tagama dashi,ni har me zaki fada in yarda dake?nima fa ba kyaleni kikayi ba,wai macen dazataje ta hadani da uwata tamin sharri akan abinda bansan hawa ba bansan sauka,nasan karya take itama tasan nasan karya take,wai kuma itace zata fadi wannan shashancin tayi tsammanin zan yarda da ita,tabdi ada kenan"yace aranshi tareda murmushi afili,lokacin yayi daidai dajin karar shigowar sako wayarshi daukowa yayi ya duba,yaga Aunty ce ya bude"Sallama yagani,sannan yan gaishe gaishe,yusuf inata kira bana samunka ya kuke dafatan kowa kalau"a take yatura mata ansa"Duk muna nan kalau Alhamdulillah kituro min address dinki don Allah"ya tura don zancen ba na waya bane,ko minti biyar baayi ba kuwa ta turo mishi da ansa
Jira yayi yayi sallar maghrib sannan ya fita batareda yafadawa farida cen zaije ba gudun masifa da balai, don ba yadda baiyi da ita ba akan tabashi adress din Auntyn tun ba yau ba kememe tahana,har wayo yadinga mata yana yan dabaru amma kememe,ta hanashi, don ita a rayuwarta batada wani buri daya wuce ta tata iskanci da rashin mutumci abi bayanta kullum dai takasance mai gaskiya shine farin cikin ta

RUWAN DAFA KAI 86~90Na SUMAYYA DANZABUWA
"Malam wallahi ka fita harkata,kashiga hankalinka don naga alamun baka dashi,duk sanda ka kuskura kasake cewa zaka tunkareni dawannan maganar taka ta banza wallahi hukuma ce zata rabani dakai tunda bakada mutumci"tace cikeda masifa"Allah ya huci zuciyarki gimbiyata,amma ni aganina wannan ba abinda zaisa ki fusata bane,dama wai so yakan zama laifi kenan?wallahi id
"kaji na rantse da Allah yaune zan maka gargadi na karshe,kafita harkata,kakuma ja girmanka,don dai kai ba yaro bane,idan baso kake kajawa kanka da danginka baki daya masifa ba,ni na taba ganin wannan irin balain? nace maka ni matar aure ce to ka rabu dani mana,kodayake naga alamun dai ilimin addini yamaka karanci bakadashi shiyasa,"takarasa maganar tana mai bude motar tareda shigewa,ta bugo murfin  da karfi don ya matukar bata mata rai,kunna motar tayi tanaji yanata magana tabar wajen bayan ta buleshi da kura,tareda jan tsakin takaici,cikeda mamakin rashin hankali irin na mutumin
"wanna wane irin mutum ne?"yau shine karo nakusan nawa kenan yana biyota office,daga ta fito saita ganshi,kuma bakin cikinta fa fada mishi da aurenta bama sau daya ba,to meyake so?saidai kuma idan irin yan iskan garine kawai ko yan yankan kai,tasha alwashin duk sanda yasake bayyananar mata hukuma ce zata rabasu
Da haka tadinga sake sake aranta harta karasa gida,gashi taki fadawa yusuf kullum saidai ta dawo tana kunkuni,kuma dama shima yanzu bai fiya matsawa ba da lamuranta don yariga yasaba da kuncinta tunda wani lokacin haka take haka kawai babu abinda akayi zata zauna tayita bakin ciki tanajin haushi yayita rarrashinta yana lallabata tafada mishi abinda yake damunta amma kememe,idan yaci saa ne ma zatace ya kyaleta batason magana,idan kuwa tsantsan rashin mutumcin ne akanta zata iya shigewa daki ta rufo kofa yayi bugun duniyar nan bazata bude ba,to hakanne yasa yariga yasaba koda yaganta tana bakin ciki baya ko bi ta kanta,kyaleta yake ta karata harsaitazo ta kulashi don kanta,hakika hakan kuma yafara damunta don rannan ma saida tace mushi wai ta lura ya chanja kwana biyu yadaina ji da ita(kuji fa tunda yadaina daukar wulakanci,)
Yusuf dai yarasa ta inda zai bullowa alamarin nan,yarasa ta yadda zai fara bayyanawa Abu wannan lamari saboda yana tsoron yadda zata dauki abin,amma shi a iyaka tunaninshi yanata nuna mata alamu fa,amma ina ko don yarinya ce har yanzu shiyasa taki daukan haske?to ni yanzu meye mafita?"yake tambayar kanshi,wata dabarace ta fado mishi farat daya,hakan ne yasashi jin dadi,harda dariya afili,ganin matsalarshi tazo karshe zaiyi komai yadda yakeso
Ganin zaman na bata mishi lokaci ne yasashi fita,baa jima ba kuwa ya dawo da sabuwar waya galleliya kirar samsung,har screen guard yasa aka sako mata da wani case mai zuciyoyi/heart,masu alamar love,(kai abin dariya),kwala mata kira yayi ta fito cikin hanzari,dama lokacin farida bata nan amma dai kowane lokaci zata iya shigowa,"Ga wannan,na dade inaso in baki Allah bai nufa ba"yace tareda mika mata wayar,hannu biyu tasa ta karba,tashiga kallon wayar tana jujjuyata,"wai tawace?"tace cikeda rashin fahimta,yar dariyar jin dadi yayi,don duk wasu lamuranta idan tanayi birgeshi takeyi shi baiki ba yasata agaba yayita kallonta(oh!ashedai idan kanason mutum tsakaninka da Allah wato,kyau bashida wani amfani)"shine abinda yake cewa aranshi akoda yaushe,ganin yayi shiru sai murmushi yake bai bata ansa ba yasa ta kara karfin halin tambaya,"wannan din wai tawace?"tasake cewa,cikin sassanyat muryarta mai narkar da zuciyar masoyinta yusuf,"takice,saboda nasan kina bukatarta,tunda dole zaman hakan ya dameki ko?"yace da ita cikin wata murya dashi kanshi baisan yanada ita ba,(hmm wato dai mutum yakan zama shashasha idan yana tareda wanda yakeso kenan?"),dan murmushi Abu tayi amma duk "saurin shiru yayi ganin zai wuce gona da iri,(yusuf meye haka kuma?maintain mana,kafara abu tiryan tiryan kuma kana nema ka bata aikinka,ayi komai step by step kar yarinyar nan tafara wani tunani wata zuciyar tace),"samari kuma?,ai ni banida saurayi"Cewar Abu,don ita tunda take ma bata taba saurayi ba,bayan kuwa Allah yamata baiwar farinjini,kawai dai ita dince bata samu wanda yamata ba,kuma burin iyayenta suga tadan zurfafa karatunta na boko itama,ko watarana Allah zaisa tazama wani abin arayuwa,duba da yadda rayuwar nan tazama,dukda dai ansha son hadata aure musamman a dangi,da yanuwa masu sa ido amma abubuwa basa yiwuwa saboda bataso,wani mugun dadi yaji,har yaso ya fallasa kanshi don kasa boye murmushinshi yayi,wannan tambayace da yadade yana jiran ansarta Allah ya taimakeshi yasamu yau,shikenan yanzu yasan bashida aboki/abokan takara shi kadai zaici karanshi ba babbaka,ganin yadda ya kura mata ido baya ko kiftawa ne yasata fara nuna alamun fa tanaso ta tashi,hakan ne yasashi dan saita kanshi,mika mata kwalin wayar yayi,dasu chaja da headphones daduk sauran tarkacen wayar,"gashi idan akwai wani abu dabaki gane ba gameda wayar akwai user guide aciki saiki duba,shikenan zaki iya tafiya"yace,godiya tadingayi yana cewa ai bakomai,sannan ta shige ciki,bawai don yanason ta tafi ba yabari ta tafi sai don kawai lura dayayi tana cikin wani hali
"oh ni Abu wannan wane irin mutum ne mai kirki haka,inda ace irinsu zasu yawaita ai da anji dadi,mutum babu ruwanshi,bai dauki duniya abakin komai ba Allah sarki Baban Amin,"tace tareda neman gefen gado inda Amin yake kwance yana sanaarshi ta bacci tazauna,"yau nice da irin wannan wayar danake ganin mutanen da suka isa da ita,nikam wacece ni? RUWAN DAFA KAI 91~95Na SUMAYYA DANZABUWA
"Banason kukan nan yana damuna"shine abinda yayita yiwa Abu yawo aka tanata nanatawa,"haka baban Amin ya damu da ita dama?to ya akayi ma yasan tayi kuka dazu,ko yasan halinda take ciki ayanzu?meyasa zai damu da ita??haka dai tadinga tunane tunane duk tabi tashiga wani hali don ta ma kasa fuskantar yanayin dakuma abinda ke shirin  faruwa,ta bangaren yusuf shima yanacen yanata kallon wayar yana jiran reply dinta amma shiru,"ko tayi baccine bata gani ba,ko kuwa dai dagaske bata iya karatun ba bare rubutun yadda yake tunani?"kai Allah yasa dai bahaka ba,don zanso mudan zanta a darennan konayi bacci mai dadi"yace aranshi tardeda saddaqarwa tunda ankusa minti goma aha biyar da tura sakon nashi amma shiru hakan ne yasashi tunanin duk yadda akayi tayi bacci,yana shirin ajiye wayar ya kwanta  ne yaga message yashigo"Nagode sosai Allah ya saka da alkhairi"wani mugun dadi yaji aranshi tabbas yayi underestimating yarinyar nan,bai zata takai haka ba,dubada yadda ta tsaro rubutun babu ko kuskure aciki,spelling da komai daidai,tabbas hakan ya matukar birgeshi,ita kuwa Abu saboda rashin sabo dakyar ta rubuto message din saboda wayace dabata saba da ita ba kuma karonta ne nafarko shiyasa  ta wahala,amma dole a sannu zata saba komai lokacine,"Amin,saida safe kiyi bacci Allah yatashemu lafiya"ya tura mata,itadai kasa reply tayi duk wani iri take ganin abin,saboda abune dabata taba tsammani ba ace mutum mai ilimi dan gayu,mai kudi kyakkyawan namiji irin yusuf yana nuna mata wannan kulawar a matsayinta na maiaikinsu shida iyalinshi itada ba yar kowan kowa ba,tasan dai mutumin kirki ne a iyakar zaman datayi agidan saboda ita kanta tasan yadda yake shanye wulakanci da rashin mutumci irin na farida duk hakurinta(Abun)wani lokacin gani take inda itace shi saita dinga maida martani amma inaa baya taba daukan mataki kamar wanda aka asirce,hasalima idan tana masifar baya biye mata,sau dayawa saidai ya girgiza kai yace Allah ya kyauta,duk tana lura dahakan ita,to wannan halayyar ita tasa take mishi kallon kamilin mutum mai mutumci da hakuri,gashida rikon ibada,bakuma yataba nunawa ita maiaiki  ce sabanin yadda farida take nuna mata kamar ma ita din wata halitta ce ta daban
Yusuf yanacen yana jiran reply,ya juya ya kalli farida da ta dade da shanya  hakora sai minshari take,harda  yawun bacci,murmushi yayi dabaima san dalilin yin hakan ba kawai dai yasan ya tsinshi kanshi cikin wani sabon yanayi,cigaba  yayi da latsa wayarshi,"Allah yabamu Allhairi ya tashemu lafiya"yaga Abu ta turo,murmushi yayi a fili harda washe hakora kamar tana gabanshi yana ganinta,sai yanzu kwakwalwarshi ta nusantar dashi dalilin dadewar yarinyar  wajen yimishi reply nacewar bata saba da waya bane shiyasa,"Allah sarki dasannu dai,"yasha alwashin zai dinga yawan mata message yadda zata koyi typing dasauri,yakuma wayar da ita ahankali,dahaka ya ajiye wayar ya kwanta yayi baccin dadi cikeda farinciki da nishadi
Har mafarki yayi wai sunyi aure suna shan soyayya
Haka lamura suka dinga kasancewa kullum idan yusuf baya gida yakan kira Abu sau ba adadi kafin yadawo acewar wai yana kira ne yaji idan komai lafiya,musamman Amin,tun bata iya sakin jiki suyi hira harsuka fara sabawa yau da gobe sai Allah,itama kuma idan taga bai kira ba kamar  yadda yasaba sai ta fara damuwa to amma ko meyasa oho?wannan tambayace datasha tambayar kanta amma dai har yanzu takasa samun ansa
Farida nashigowa gida yau ta hango Su Abu akan tabarma itada Amin,gawani mutum akan kujera azaune,da alamun dai karatu sukeyi,tunda ga Quranai nan ahannayensu,kwafa tayi cikeda rashin fahimtar abinda ke faruwa ma,parking tayi  ta fito cikeda masifa da balai a tattare da ita tacika ta batse nema take kawai ta fashe,yusuf yanajin  shigowarta yayi saurin fitowa don yasan yanzu saita iya aikata abinda  bashikenan ba ta tapka rashin mutumci,"Baby"yadan kirata tajiyo ta zabga mshi wata harara don tabbas da saninshi ake wannan lamarin,"meye?"ta bashi ansa"bismillah shigo daga ciki"yace tareda wangame mata kofar,  ganin harta nufi inda suke karatun,"kamarya inshigo daga ciki meke faruwa ne,waye wannan din?"tace fuskar nan cikeda iko da mulki,"kishigo  mana don Allah zan miki bayani"yusuf din yace  cikin kasa kasa da murya kamar mai munafurci wai don Kar malam din yajisu,tsaki taja cikeda takaici,kafin ta ankara sai ganin yusuf tayi yakamo hannunta yashige da ita ya rufo kofar,binshi kawai tadingayi da ido cikeda mamaki,"sakeni mana meye haka zaka wani kamoni kamar wata yarinya agaban yara"tace a hasale,"toh nasakeki"yace bayan ya saki hannun nata,jakarta ta wurgar akan kujera hadeda key din"kayimin  bayanin abinda ke faruwa acen"tace cikin  masifa  tareda nuni da inda su Abu suke karatun  ta window tunda ana hangosu,"karatu sukeyi mana"yabata ansar a takaice bayan yanemi waje yazauna,"wat?kamarya karatu islamiyyar kuma fa?ko tafi karfin taje islamiyyar tunda ta shahara,?"takara cikeda rashin fahimta,"babu laifin yarinyar nan,laifina ne,amma kinsandai koba komai yarinyar  nan amana ce agaremu ko?gani nayi masu gadin unguwarnan dawasu en iska na daban,suna neman su sa mata ido kowa fa yasakata agaba"saboda ga Aishwarya Rai ko?wannan harwani kyau ne da ita dazaawani sakata agaba?meye wani abin birgewa a tattare da ita dagar zai wani ja hankalin namiji?kodayake duk meye dama daidai dasu suka gani shiyasa"tayi maganar cikeda izgili,yusuf baiji dadin zancen ba amma dai ya dake saboda bashida ikon nuna bacin ranshi a yanzu,"duk abar wannan,zancen ai ba sai mace tanada kyau maza suke binta ba,farin jini ma ai is something,to cut it short dai saboda gudun kada sani abu yazo yafaru mara dadi,shiaysa kawai naga gwara in samo mata mai mata karatun  agida tunda baa hanata karatu ba sharadin mama ne,"kallonshi kawai take tunda yafara maganar har yakai aya,wata yar dariya tayi wadda duk wanda yagani yasan  tarainin hankali ce,"wannan ne kawai dalilin?nace wannan ne kawai silly reason din?wai kai me kake nufi ne da lamarin yarinyar nan?yusuf the rate at which kafara zakewa akan mai aikin nan kuma yana nenan yafara bani haushi  fa,ina ruwanka da sabgarta ko kana mantawa  ne da kalamanka na baya?kuma ma ni danake da iko da ita shikenan ban isa  kafadamin abu ba saidai kawai inga ka aikata?ko kana mantawa nima gidan nan nawa ne?ta inda take shiga bata nan take fita ba ta mugun fusata taji haushi,yusuf yasan bai kyauta ba wannan karon tunda da gaskiyarta ko ba komai itama ai tanada iko bai kamata kawai ace taga abuba bazata to amma kuma me?tsakani da Allah yasan halinta babu yadda zaayi yafada mata kudirinshi akan hakan ta yarda shiyasa yanke hukuncin Koda Abu taga sakon saida zuciyarta tabada wani daram don ta dade tana shan jinin jikinta akan hakan amma kuma bataso ta tabbatar ita ya zatayi yanzu?,"mamaki ne yahanaki turomin ansa ko kinyi bacci?"yasake tura mata,"to yazaayi ma yace yana sontawai,?wannan wane irin so ne?yusuf yafi karfinta nesa ba kusa ba,shiyasa kenan duk wanda zaizo neman aurenta, saiya koreshi ashe yanada nashi kudirin,ya ilahi,wayyo Baban Amin meyasa yafara sonta alhalin ita tasan bazata taba sonshi ba,ita da ahalin daake ciki ma batasan metake ji ba game dashi don bata taba doyayya ba baretasani ko tafara sonshi ne itama ko kuwa akasin haka,kuma ma duk abar ta wannan tayaya zasuyi zaman kishiyoyi itada farida?farida fa?idan aka cire masifarta da bakin halinta,macece iyaka macece,don Abu rabonda taga mace mai kyau haka tamanta,indai ba yanada wata manufa ba tashi takanshi me zaiyi da ita?me matarshi ta rasa da ita zata iya bashi?wasu hawayene masu zafi suka fara zubo mata don hakika tana cikin tsaka mai wuya,wannan wane irin abu ne?ya zaayi tana yar aikin gida maigida yace yanasonta?me mutane zasu dinga tunani akanta kenan?taci amana?daga zuwa aiki ta kwace mijin matar gida?labarin datakeji yau kanta ya fado kenan?agaskiya bazata iya ba gwara ma idan barin gidan ne tayi
Ganin shirun yayi yawane yasa yusuf dan shiga damuwa amma shima dama yasan dole zaayi haka ai  don abune dabata taba zata ba,kasa nutsuwa yayi dole yasauke kan farida dake kirjinshi tana ta minshari harda yawun bacci yafita palon saman don kiran Abu,saida ya kira sau uku tana tsinkewa ana hudun tadauka yanajin muryarta yasan sanaar tata take ta kuka,"don Allah kiyi hakuri zainab nasan abinnan yazo miki bazata amma wallahi dagaske nake tsakanina da Allah nake son ki kasnce matata wallahi ban fada miki abinnan ba don in bata miki rai"kuka tafashe dashi,wanda harsaida tadan ruufe bakinta donkarta tashi Amin,"kiyi hakuri kidaina kukan nan kinsan banaso yana damuna kicemin wani abu ko naji dadi"yace a marairaice,dakyar ta iya hadiye kukan tafara magana,"nagode da kulawarka da soyayyar dakace kana min amma bazan iya aurenka ba baban Amin"kafin yayi magana takashe wayargabaki daya kiran duniyar nan wayar akashe, dole ya hakura yakoma daki yakwanta cikeda damuwa yanata fatan Allah yasa dai ta aminta dashi don shi yanzu idan tace bazata aureshi ba baisan yazaiyi ba tabbas yariga yagama macewa da sonta hakika zai shiga wani hali

Farida tana office tana mita cikeda takaici da bakin cikin sammy tashigo ta isketa,"mekuma ya faru?"nan ta kwashe duk yadda sukayi da yusuf awaya yanzu,tafada mata nacewar Amin yafara magana,kuma wai sunan mai aiki yafara fada shine abin bakincikinta,dariya sammy ta kyalkyale da ita,"to ke meye abin jin haushi tsakani da Allah,yaron nan fa daake zance tun yana jariri rabonki dashi to meye kuma don yafara fadar sunan uwarshi ta biyu?kema dai kinada abin mamaki ai yaro yana fara magana ne  da fadar abinda yafiji dakuma wayanda suke ataredashi akoda yaushe"cewar sammy tareda neman waje tazauna,"ni bakin cikina shine yaron nan bama sunan babanshi yafara fada ba ni dama bance ni ba,kowani abu mai muhimmanci sammy sunan mai aiki?"tace cikeda kulewa da tsantsar bakinciki,"to wai dazaki isheni ita ba mutum bace?kuma dai naga ke kika dau ragamarshi gabaki daya rankatakaf kika danka mata kamar fa bata shi kekayi to what do you expect dama?haba hajiya ai kawai ki rungumi kaddara kizubawa sarautar Allah ido tunda kece sanadin faruwar komai,"haka dai farida tayita mita sammy na kallonta don jinta kawai take, saboda idan tafara mita  zatayita zance daya ne har sai mutum yagaji ya kyaleta

"kuka yaci karfinta ta kasa karasa zancen,"kiyi hakuri kinji nima nakanyi mamakin hakan,amma bakomai kinsan dai da raina da lafiyata bazan bari wani yace zai  muzguna muku ba ko?"gyada kai tayi alamun eh"yawwa to so nake ki kwantar da hankalinki,ni mai kaunarku ne a kullum kuma abinda kukeso shi zaayi,zan kirashi gobe akan ya janye maganar auren idan yace bazai janye ba to ya zama dolene yabaki takardarki ,bazan laminci wannan harkar tsiyar ba harkar talauci,ace wai mai aikinki ce zata zama kishiyarki"nagode Abba,wallahi kai mai kaunatane a kullum ni nasani kamin komai"tace cikin kuka,"tabbas ni mai kaunarku ne a kullum,in ban kaunaceku ba waye zai kaunace ku,ki share hawayenki kibar kukan nan haka kar kije kanki yadinga ciwo,duk abinda kukeso a duniyar nan shi zakuyi,jeki kwanta saida safe"sallama sukayi tashige,amma koda ta kwanta kasa baccin tayi sai juye juye data dinga yi tana kukan bakin ciki wai ita yusuf zai musgunawa?abinda bata taba tunani ba ko a mafarki,shikenan sai su dinga sharing dinshi kenan itada Mai aiki?tabbas hakan bazai taba yiwuwa ba,bazata taba raba miji dawata mace ba kowacece ita kuwa,dahaka dai har tayi bacci

Dan kwanciya yayi, baisan sanda bacci yadaukeshi ba,Sai farkawa yayi yaga gari yayi haske har tara tayi,jin dan motsi yayi abayanshi,saida yadan tsorata don shidai yasan ba farida bace,to waye a gadon,ahankali ya juyo yaga Amin,yanata bacci abinshi cikeda kwanciyar hankali don saida tamishi wanka tashiryashi sannan ta lallabashi yayi bacci ta kawoshi don karyaga tafiyarta yayi rigima,"aa me yaron nan yake anan?ya akayi ma yazo?"yafara tambayar kanshi,juyawarshi keda wuya yaga yar takarda A kan bedside drawer,adan danne da waya,kodaya duba wayar  Abu yagani,ai arikice ya tashi,cikeda fatan Allah yasa dai ba abinda yake tunani bane,"bude takardar yayi yaga rubutu kamar haka"Assalam Alaikum Baban Amin,ina fatan abinda zan fada maka yazama maslaha ga dukkanin fitintinun dana tsundumaku aciki,ni Abu na tafi garinmu don bazan iya cigaba da zama agidanku ba,kuna rayuwarku cikin haske sakamakon zuwana kuka shiga duhu,don Allah kuyafemin don nasan nice silar komai,nagode da soyayyarka dakuma kyautatawarka agareni,Allah yahadamu da  Alkhairin shi Amin"wata ajiyar zuciya ya saki tareda dafe kanshi"wato yarinyar nan dai dagaske taken kenan saida ta gudu,aikuwa ko birnin  sin ta tafi wallahi saiya nemota ya aureta,zataga karshen naci,tunda ya fuskanci batasan menene so ba,batasan kuma  soyayyar dayake mata tafi karfin wasa ba bazai yiwu ba ta ajiye mishi wannan  yar takardar tayi tunanin shikenan wannan dan rubutun ya isa yasa ya  manta da ita ba wasa ma ake kenan

RUWAN DAFA KAI 111~115Na SUMAYYA DANZABUWA
Gidan Hajiya  suka wuce kai tsaye don ko gidan nashi ma baya shaawar komawa don bayason wani abu dazai tuna mishi da farida kwata kwata,so yake yafitar da ita daga zuciyarshi da rayuwarshi baki daya  ko ta halin kaka tunda yariska ce ita batada mutumci,don duk macen dazata ce zata raina mahaifiyar mutum ko wacece ita to kuwa batada wani sauran amfani,bare shi dababu abinda yake darajawa sama da mahaifiyarshi a rayuwa,tabbas kuwa duk wanda yace zai bata mata dole shima ya bata mishi
Ganin halinda ya shiga ne harda su kin cin abinci,yasa Hajiyar zaunar dashi tafara mishi nasiha,tana kwantar mishi da hankali akan Allah zai bashi wadda ta fita inshaallah,wannan bawani abin damuwa bane,farida tariga ta tafka babban kuskure amma bakomai kanta tayiwa ai gani take gata yamata yawa  rayuwa ce ba tabbas yau da gobe sai Allah,"Allah ma yabani inshaallah  don yariga yabani zainab"cewarshi,cikin wata murya mai ban tausayi,dan murmushi hajiya tayi,"lallai wannan Zainab kanaji da ita,Allah yasa yadda ka damu da ita haka ta damu dakai itama"amin"yabada ansa
(A yau nayi niyyar  binta don hankalinshi yakasa kwanciya so yake dai ya tabbatarda gidan taje,kar wani abu yasameta,amma Hajiya ta hanashi tace yabari sai gobe don bazata bari ko fita yayi a yau ba bare yayi tuki zuwa waje mai nisa dubada irin halinda yake ciki)
"wallahi inda nasan Irin wulakancin Dazanje in tarar agidansu Farida kenan da banje ba"kabar maganar nan don Allah,kuma ai kai nutsatse ne mai tarbiyya mahaifinta ya kiraka sai kace bazaka ba ko me?kada wannan abinda yafaru yasa ka chanja halaye yusuf kaji,nasanka mutum ne mai nutsuwa da Hankali,da tsantsar hakuri kacigaba ahaka inshaallah bazaka taba ganin ba daidai  ba arayuwarka kaji"cewar Hajiya cikin rarrashi,"Hajiya meye amfanin zuwan yanzu, kina gani fa banda cimana mutumci babu sukayi  wai harni mahaifinta zaice zai biya kudin motocina da ta lalata?,inda yasan damages din da yarinyar nan tamin arayuwa
"ya isa mana,nace ya isa yusuf ina hakurinka ne?"kuka ya fashe dashi,hakan ne yasa zuciyar Hajiya karyewa itama don tasan ba karamin abu bane yakesa yusuf dinta kuka tun yana karami,mutum ne mai tsantsan hakuri amma akwai juriya,dole ta kyaleshi ya fitar da bakincikin dake cikin zuciyarshi daya dade yana kunsa"agaskiya natapka babban kuskure tun farko da nabari so ya rufemin ido nakasaganin abubuwa tuntuni,babu irin zantukan dabaa kawomin ba akan yarinyar nan amma nadinga sharewa ina kauda kai saboda ni aganina duk karyane,sharri ne,amma tunda na auri yarinyar nan cikin bakin ciki nake,wallahi nayi danasanin auren far
"meyasa kake zance hakane yusuf,kana mantawa da kaddara ne,Allah yariga yarubuta dole sai kunzauna  gashi harda rabon da sai kuma kadinga yiwa  kaddara musu?kabar zancennan haka don Allah ya isa,"share hawayenshi yayi Hajiya nabinshi da kallo cikeda tausayinshi,"fatana dai shine Allah yasa ita zainab din ta kasance mace ta gari dazata share maka hawaye"Amin yace
Ganin shiru danuwansu dansanda bai kirata ba gameda wani bayani akansu  gloria ne yasa ta kirashi,inda ya tabbatar mata dacewar sufa sunyi iyaka abinda zasuyi amma babu alamun wayannan yaran datake fada,suna tunanin dai guduwa sukayi duk yadda akayi,hakan baiyi mata dadi ba tabbas don duk yadda taso taga ta sake sashi wani aikin abin yaci tura shikuwa  yariga yagano bakin zaren sarai  ya fuskanci sharri ne takeson hadawa duk yadda akayi,don baya raba dayan biyu,watakila wani abune ya hadata dasu takeson hukuntasu ta wannan hanyar,ko kuma dai wani dalilin cen nata na daban,amma a yadda sukayi bincike sukagano cewar yaron masu aiki ne babu yadda zaayi suyi taammali da hodar iblis din(cocaine)don tafi karfinsu basuda kudin dazasuyi harka da ita,hakuri kawai yabata yakashe wayarshi don baisan mezai mata ba
Wata ashar ta kunduma,"ni zai kashewa waya?lallai ma dadinta dai bashi kadai bane dan sanda agarinnan,yana nufin bazai ma iya komai ba kenan sai anyi magana yafi kowa katon bakin cewa shi dansanda ne ya iya aikinshi,mutum sai kuri,aikin banza aikin hofi shashashan banza,babu wanda zaka Iya huce haushi dashi aduniyar ma ,"ta ja tsaki
Washegari yusuf yana tashi ya shirya sukaci Abinci shida Amin,daya tarar Hajiya ta shirya shi shima,an saka mishi kayan daya daga cikin jikokin gidan,dasuke bari in sunzo,(tunda babu shiri sukazo),Sallama yayiwa Hajiya suka kama  hanyar Jigawa, da har zai kira Bashir ya rakashi sai kuma dai ya kyaleshi ganin cewar bai sanar dashi tunda wuri ba watakila yanada nashi uzurin tunda yau asabar
Koda suka isa Gumel din baiwani bata lokaci ba yafara tambayar Kauyen su Abu,dayake sanannen kauye ne bai wani sha wahalar kwatance ba,amma fa akwai nisa,da tambaya Allah ya taimaka ya isa,lokacin har anyi Azahar
Ba bata lokaci yafara tambayar gidan Liman,cikin saa kuwa yasamu wani yaro,irin yan dadi motar nan dason zuwa birni yace zai rakashi har gidan,ko tsoron asaceshi ma baiji ba yashige motar cikeda murna
Basu tsaya ko ina ba sai kofar gidan,"ka tabbata nanne gidan dai ko?"Cewar yusuf,"eh nan ne wallahi""to kashiga kace Abu tazo","to"yace cikin jin dadi da hanzari,har yayi gaba yusuf ya kirashi yadawo,"karbi wannan kasai alawa"ya karbe kudin ba ko godiya yashiga aguje don tsananin murnar an danashi a mota,mahaifiyarta Hadiza wadda suke kira da gwaggo ya tarar a tsakar gidan tana duba girki,sallama ya rapka ta ansa,"wai ance Abu tazo"har lokacin yanata murna abindai sai wanda yagani,"kai kuwa dadina dakai bala shashanci,baka iya ko gaisuwa ba,anma ci saa dai yau kayi sallama, waye yake nemanta?"wani mutumine dayazo a mota,dan birni""a mota kuma?"ta nanata cikeda rashin fahimta,Abu dake dakintana jiyo duk abinda ake gabanta  ne yabada wani ras,badai biyota mutumin nan yayi ba?"kwala mata kira mahaifiyar tata yayi,ta fito "wane mai mota ne yazo nemanki?"nima bansani ba"tace cikeda rashin fahimta"kinsan dai mutanen yanzu abin tsorone ni wallahi b
"sallamar Liman ce ta katsemata zance,ga hannun dan yaro ya kamo"ai Amin yana ganin uwarshi yasaki hannun liman ya ruga wajenta aguje itama haka,cikeda murna ta dagashi sama suna haukansu dasuka saba,saijin dadi yaron yake,"Zan shigo kenan nahadu dawani bako a waje yacemin shine maigidan da abu tayi aiki cen kano,ta taho ne jiya baisani ba,shine ya biyo sahu yaga ko ta iso lafiya wannan yaronshi ne"cewar Baba tareda nuni da Amin"wato saida yabiyoni kenan?kaini wannan wane irin  mutum ne kamar yana mantawa da masifaffiyar matarshi","Allah sarki hanata fita kikayi kenan kinajin tsoro"yace yana dan dariya bayan tafadamishi yadda sukayi da Bala,"to Malam ba dole ba kasan mutane yanzu abin tsoro ne"ke kuma  ki dauki ruwa  ki kaimishi mana  daga gani yasha hanya,kuma gashi tsaye cikin rana""toh"ta Ajiye Amin wanda duk inda tayi yana binta don karta kara guduwa ta barshi,"lallai wannan yaro yana kaunarki haka kuka saba?"cewar gwaggo ganin shakuwar tayi yawa tsakanin maiaiki dai da yaron gida,"dan murmushi tayi don inda sunsan tarihin yaron nan dasunsha mamaki mara misaltuwa, dan dakin daake  ajiye kayan girki(kitchen)irin nasu na kauye,ta shiga ta dauko dan jug irin na robar nan mai hadeda kofinanshi, na baki ta dora akan dan paranti kamar baa kauye ba,komaidai mai tsabta da dan wayewa daidai su,dama da hijabinta ajikinta,ta nufi waje,Amin na biye,su Baba sunata mamaki suna dariya
Tana isa soro ta rage sauri taje ta dan leka a hankali waidai ta tabbatar,ganinshi tayi tsaye jikin mota ga rana na haskashi,sai kuma kawai taji wata tsananin  kunyarshi,tunda take ma ita bata taba kunyarshi  ba irin yau,"tana leke leken ne Baba yafito da tabarma a hannu,"aa ya hakane?me kike tun dazu baki kai ruwan ba laben nameye?"aa ba labewa nayi ba hijabina nake gyarawa"tacebayan tadan saita fuskar hijabin,"to maza kawo ruwan,"Baba ya karbi parantin ya ajiye akan tabarmar daya shimfida" ki fita kice yashigo nan,wajen da rana ai"(kunsan bakauyen mutum da karrama bako mashaallah)" fita tayi cikin sanyin jiki,kamar wadda kwai yafashewa aciki tadinga tafiya  har ta isa inda yake,shi baima kula da fitowar tata ba,yana latsa waya kasancewar sunada service a garin,"wai kashigo ciki"juyowa yayi jin muryar ta dayayi missing kwana biyu,sannan yadanyi murmushi,"Wato wai in shigo ciki ko?ke dai ba ke kikaso ba kenan wai ne abin"yace fuskarshi daukeda farincikin ganinta,sunkuyi dakai tayi don inta  hada ido dashi wani iri takeji,"baba ne yace kashigo"tasake cewa batareda ta kalleshi ba,"to zan shigo"yace,gaba sukayi itada danta,yana binsu abaya har  suka shiga,takalmanshi yacire yadare kan tabarma,itakuma ta kama hanya zata shige,"waike baki iya tarbar bako bane ko gaisheni bakiyi ba,bawani irin dan nuna murnar nan irinta kinga masoyin nan naki,wajenki fa nazo zaki wani tafi ki barni"yayi maganar cikeda zolaya,"wai masoyi,wajena kuma?"tananata aranta take wata kunyarshi tasake lullubeta,"bazaa dai a kulani ba kenan ni zaa jawa aji ko? Bakomai kowa da lokacinshi"Ganin maganganinshi dai bazasu kare ba sukuma  daina saka ta jin kunya ne yasa tashige gida,suna shiga ta wucesu baba a tsakar gida suka shige daki,"ke wai saurin nameye haka kamar an biyoki?yanzu haka kika bar bakon  shi kadai"cewar gwaggo,"kinsan halin mutuniyartaki  ai"toh malam nidai Allah  yasa bawani abin tamisu ba acen din",cewar gwaggo cikeda damuwa,"don tunda tadawo nayi nayi tafadi  dalilin dawowarta taki tace ganin gida tazo,kuma gashi shi cemaka yayi ta taho basu sani ba bansan sanda Abu tafara karya ba kuma,"haba bakomai ma inshaallah,don bana tunanin wani abu tayi gaskiya,ni aganina inda tamusu wani abu ne muna haduwa zai sanar dani,amma baicemin komai ba faran faran muka gaisa gaskiya yaron akwai hankali kamar ba irin yan birnin nan ba "baba yace,"Hakane,Allah yasa to"Amin bari inje mugaisa dakyau"ya zura takalmanshi yayi soro
Bayan sun gaisa ne Baba yake tambayar Allah yasa dai komai lafiya bawani abu tayi musu cen dinba,ai tun kafin yakai Aya yusuf ya tari numfashinshi  akan babu abinda ta aikata sai allhairi,ba bata lokacin yafara yabonta,yana yaba irin kyawun tarbiyyarta  da halayenta nagari,"toh mashaallahu haka akeso ai ai Abu ko annan  dinma ana yabon halayenta matuka yarinya ce mai nutsuwa da hankali batada hayaniya samsam"baba ya kara,saida duk aka gama wannan lamarin sannan yusuf yayiwa bbaba bayanin komai  akanshifa tsakaninshi da Allah yakeson Abu kuma da aure,take ya kwashe mishi duk abubuwan dasuka  faru  tsakaninshi da farida bai karaba baikuma rage komai ba don bazai iya yiwa surikinshi karya ba,"kai wanna abu baiyi dadi ba ,to inba ma dai abu irin na mace ba,don miji yace zai kara aure sai rigima har akaiga rabuwa,kai gaskiya rabuwar aure batada da dadi sam sam,mu data dawo nan babu irin tambayar dabamuyi ba don abin babu zato ba tsammani,amma kememe taki fadar dalili"dan murmushi yusuf yayi,"Ai tanada hankali ne da nutsuwa matuka nasan bazata fada ba dama,shiyasa nace dole in biyo sahu,Allah yasa dai mudace kawai"yusuf yadinga cewa baba yanata bayani,"lamarin abu kuma gaka gata,don mu nan bamayiwa yara auren dole gaskiya,baa tursasa yarinya ta auri wanda bata so, idan ta amince dakai wallahi mu bamuda wata matsala kuma dazarar munyi bincikenmu akanka muntabbatar da halayenka na kirki,saidai muyi fatan Allhairi amma idan bata amince dakai ba saidai mubaka hakuri,yasunan Bakon namu ne"yusuf ne Baba"yace,"toh toh,mashaallah malam yusuf"hakane baba,tadade da amincewa dani ai, taku amincewar dai nake nema kawai, don ita tabani kwarin gwiwa ma wajen ganin nazo nasameka"yace,"to to,kai kaji yara wato kunma dade da daidaita kanku kenan,To Alah yasa albarka yasa damu zaayi,"yayi dan murmushi,nan suka dan  taba hira kasancewar baba mutum ne mai ilimin addini da babu ruwanshi faran faran
kwanon abincin baki gwaggo ta zuba wa yusuf sannan ta kwala mata kira ta zo"gashi kikaiwa  bakon,wai ya sunanshi nema?"hijabinta taja tarufe  ido wai kunya"yau naga abu ni Dije wai meye hakane?tunda bawan Allah nan yazo kike shakiyanci zaki fadamin sunan nashi  ko kuwa?"cewar gwaggo tana yar dariya,don tariga ta fuskanci inda yar tata ta dosa,"Yusuf"tace dakyar harda wani murmushi,murmushi itama gwaggon  tayi,"kije ki dawo zaki zo kimin bayani ne tunda kema wai kin iya gulma har ni zaki boyewa abu ko?"dariya tayi kawai ta dauki parantin,gimtse dariyar tata tayi data karasa soron ta ajiye mishi abinci ta tashi zata juya ne baba ya dakatar da ita yamata bayanin duk abinda yusuf yazo dashi,"Au yanzu maman  Amin saida tasa yasaketa?  Ni dabata ma ga na amince dashi ba kai wannan mata akwai jahilar mace"kinyi shiru bakice  komai ba baba ya katse mata tunani,kallon fuskar yusuf tayi saikuma duk yabata tausayi gaskiya ya cancanci  ta soshi,ko don Abinda farida tamishi,kuma ma wane kykkyawan dan birne ne mai ilimi irinshi zaice yanason irinta yar kauye har ya gwammace ya rabu  da matarshi saboda ita gashi har ya iya jurewa ya biyota kauyen nan nasu mai mugun nisa,bai taba kyamatarta  ba kasancewarta yar talaka dabatada komai,yasan matarshi tafita komai  amma yazabeta ahaka,gaskiya yusuf ya cancanshi ta kyautata mishi don ita tunda  take bata taba gani ko jin labarin namiji irinshi ba,idan tace batasonshi ma a
"Kunyarce wai  duk haka?"baba ya katsemata tunani,ganin tayi shiru ta kalli kasa,nan kuwa baisan abubuwa bane suke mata yawo a cikin kanta kala kala,kallon shi  tayi ya sakar mata wani murmushin daya kashe mata jiki harda kifta mata ido,batasan sanda ta mayar mishi murmushin ba,dasauri ta tashi tayi cikin gida aguje,hakan ne ya tabbatarwa da Baba cewar ta amince dai kenan,"to Allah ya tabbatar da alkhairi yasa damu zaayi"Amin"inji yusuf,ya bude Abincin shinkafa da wake ne da mai,yazuba abinshi yafara ci
Tare sukaje masallacin da baban ya ke limanci don gabatar da sallar laasar,inda aka dinga haduwa da yan gari baba yana gabatar  dashi a matsayin wanda yakeson Ya auri Abu,kunsaidai rayuwar duniya duk inda ka kai da abinka saika sami makiya da mahassada,irin yan samarin nan dasuka sha cewar suna son Abu tana kinsu sai kishi da bakin ciki,aka fara gulma ana cewa dama kwadayi yamata yawa ta rainasu ne shiyasa takisu,gashi saida taje birni tasamo mai kudi,wasu kuma suce duk muninta amma wannan ya yarda zai aureta ko ina  ruwansu oho?,haka sauran yanmatan gari dasukaji labari aka dinga munafurci ana maida zance tunda ita ko kawa ma bata da ita saboda mutum ce dabatason hayaniya da tashin hankali kullum inbata gida tana makaranta,musamman aka dinga zuwa har kofar gidan ana ganin yusuf,tabbas ranar celebrity yazama
Koda suka shiga gida lekawa Baba yayi yaceda gwaggo ta leko su gaisa zai tafi
Bayan sunyi sallama ne ya dan leko yaga mutanen sun tattafi,an watse hakan ne yasashi ajiyar zuciya yanufi mota,yazauna jiran fitowarta don yasan zata kawo amin dole,itama leke leken tafarayi don Gudun idon mutane,sannan ta kamo hannun Amin suka nufi motar,bude mata dayan side din yayi yamata nuni alamun tashiga"da ta tsaya zata fara noke noke,tahango su Marka uwayen gulma da munafurci sun shawo kwana batasan sanda ta shige ba,"inye su Abu tawa"yace yana  mata wani  kallo,"yaushe nazama taka"tace batareda ta kalleshi ba tana yar dariya,"iyye buduri wato an dawo gabansu baba baki ya bude,madallah"yar dariya takarayi ita duk wani iri takeji,"ku tafi kar dare yayi"tace,"munki mutafi din,duk wa ya jawo muka dade?dama ai donke mukazo,saboda sonkai kika dauki danki kika shige dashi kukayita hira nikuma,aka barni nikadai ko?"to ba kunyi ba kaima kai da Baba"tace harda yar shagwaba,"hehe bidiri wallahi Zainabu su gwaggo  shagwabaki sukayi"haka yadinga janta da hira yana tsokanarta,  tana  bashi ansa daidai saboda rashin sabo don ita tunda takem   bata taba zance ba,su alawar madara,gullisuwa danginsu tsamin gaye dasauran irin tarkacen nan, gwaggo ta hadowa Amin,saisu Kuka,kubewa  kanwa,irin dai kayan girkin nan na mata Na Hajiya,"wai,wai wannan duk namu ne,to mungode kice muna yiwa Gwaggo godiya"samsung dinta S9 yadauko ya mika mata,ganin sunada  wuta agarin kuma ga service,bazata dinga rasa chargi ba,"gata nan nadawo miki da abarki",yace hadeda murmushi itama yar dariya tayi "kaiiii, dama kabarta wallahi i
"inbarta indinga jin muryarki ina ganinkinta ina?kina wasa fa da soyayata agareki yarinyar nan naga alama"yace,karba tayi ta sunkuyi dakai,"nagode"sai wannan kuma  kibawa Gwaggo don Allah naso nabata dazu sai nake tsoron kartaki karba"yace bayan ya mika mata kudi masu tarin yawa"kabarshi don Allah"saida taga yadage yace idan bata karba ba kwana zasuyi,sannanta karba,sukayi sallama akan duk sanda zai  sake dawowa zai kirata
Amin najin an fara sallama yafara rigima,"tare zamu tafi kaji,kayana zan dauko aciki"tace dashi sannan yadanyi shiru,"Allah yakiyaye"tace cikin wata murya mai kama da rada wai don kar yaron yaji,dasauri sauri tashige gida,sai lokacin ya tada mota suka kama hanya yaron yayita rigima yusuf yana rarrashinshi
Basu shigo garin kano ba sai isha dama sunyi da bash zasu hadu,gida yafara zuwa ya ajiye Amin yayi wanka yayi sallah, sannan yayiwa Hajiya bayanin duk yadda abubuwa suka faru,yakuma kawo abubuwan daaka basu yabata,inda tadinga  godiya tana fatan alkhairi
koda suka hadu labarin duk abubuwan dasuka  faru yabashi,mamaki  kamar ya kasheshi "yanzu ita faridan  da bakinta tace  kasaketa  ta saboda zaka kare aure?" ap zancen kakeso kuma ,wannan tafi karfin tunaninka fa,wani sai ya rantse bata taba ilimin addinin islama ba""agaskiya dai nayi mamaki matuka,to ai shikenan"hira suka dinga tabawa,shidai bash sai  jinjina zancen yake,"tab,daga baya kenan,ai ni nariga  nagama da lamarinta  kuma har abada Taje ta karata badai  tace na zalumceta ba na cuceta  a rayuwa harda tsinemin dajamin Allah ya isa,kai babu irin balain da yarinyar nan bata kiramin ba,haka kawai babu abinda na mata,ai nagaya mata idan ni nacuceta Allah ya saka mata idan kuma ita tacuceni Allah  yasaka min"shikenan kuwa angama magana"cewar bash,"to yanzu dai  yaushe zumusha  biki?"bawani daukan lokaci fa,nan kusa inshaallah,inaso ne  inje insamu wannan kawun  nawa in fada mishi komai tunda  mungama dasu cen  inyaso ko zuwan dazan sakeyi ne sai akai lefe asaka rana  in ta kama ma harsu  daurin aure duk ayi a huta kawai "shege,haka ka matsu dayawa?"kai daallah badama mutum yayi magana sai kayi fassara,shikenan sai in cigaba da zama haka Bayan Alla ya rufamin asiri"zakayi bayani ne,amma fa mutumima zaka hada  musu zafi fa,  abin yayi wuri dayawa,"bash kenan zafin me?badai kayan daki bane  na alada damuka  dorawa kanmu? idan zaa bimusulumci ai baace  mace ta kawowa miji  gadon dazai kwanta ba,kujerar dazai zauna,butar dazaije bandaki ko kuma kwanon abincin dazaici ba,babu inda aka tilasta haka,aladar banza ce dai kawai da akeyi ana  wahalar dakai nikam na dauke musu,don duk wani abu da iyaye suke kawo mace dashi zanyiwa zainab inshaallah"dan iska jinka kake fa kamar dangote ko?"ya son ranka"yusuf yabashi ansa,"mashaallah Allah sarki kumafa haka ya kamata,amma kabirgeni wallahi wannan aladar  batada  wani amfani sai kaga mutane na fama da kansu amma auren yarinya ya tashi duk abi atada hankali ana cin bashi don ayi kayan daki,"hmm kadai bari kawai wai ana gudun gori daga mutane,imagine,ko  lokacin  farida babu yadda banyi dasu  ba akan zan saka komai basai duk an kawo wayannan su kujerun ba dasuwani waye dinnan to suka dage sAi sunyi dole,kaga ai sai in hakura koba haka ba"hakane kam,kasan wayannan ai su sunaji da kudi,to ai shikenan Allah dai ya kyauta,yakuma nuna mana lokacin yabaku zaman lafiya,farida kam tayiwa kanta"
Cigaba sukayi  da yan hirarrakinsu suka rabu  akan cewar idan zuwa yatashi  zai fadamishi
Baba ne yakwashe duk yadda sukayi da yusuf yafadawa gwaggo tabbas  tayi farinciki kawarai don dama anata yayatawa a  kauyen ana cewa Sun hana  abu aure,saboda son abin duniya yarinya bawani kyau ba asamu a rufa mata asiri,amma harda turata birni, su kuwa ba hanata aure sukayi ba,duk samarin dasuke zuwa basuda nutsuwa babu tsayayyiwar sanaa,kuma babu wanda yamata,Allah yasa baba da iliminshi yasan meyake shiyasa ya dage akan cewar bazai mata auren dole ba kuma bazai bada ita ba ga namijin da baya sanaa,don ba gajiya yayi da ganinta ba ba naiman kai yake da yarshi ba,yayan ta ma Ahmad dayake karatu acen Jos shima dayake namiji an saka mishi ido ance yaki aure,saboda son abin duniya,sun dage sai sunyi kudi,dama kuma su biyu Allah yabawa iyayen nasu
"Allah kadai yasan me take acen birnin data tafi,yarinya ta doshi shekaru ashirin,duk tabi ta tsufa",(dududu shekarunta goma sha tara fa abun,)wannan ne  zancen mahassadan kauyen a kullum
Washegari daawuri yusuf ya tafi gida don yanaso yafara  duk wasu yan gyare gyare dazaiyi agidan  na shirin zuwan amarya
Ganin farida batada niyyar zuwa kwashe kayanta ne yasashi samo motocin kwasar kaya irin manya manyan nan,yasasu suka loda komai dayasani nata dangin furniture dasu kayan kitchen duk tarkace da shirmen banza don rabin kayan kitchen dinma baa taba amfani dasu ba,ana kwashe kayan yana mita yana tsaki cikeda takaici,"almubazzarancin banza da hofi"saida suka gama loda kayan tas yamusu kwatance suka tafi kaiwa don amintattu ne ya yarda dasu yasan babu yadda zaayi suce zasu sace kayan
Kayan sawarta kuma dasu wani sarkokinta gwala gwalai hardasu diamonds dasauransu,(abinku da yar masu kudi)su computer da duk abinda yake nata,yaloda su a akwatina da kwalaye, yasaka Malam Hamisu Direban hajiya yakaisu,kafin kuce kwabo gida yayi tas
Motocin data lalata suma yasa akazo aka kwashesu don saida gidan ma zaiyi,dama akwai gini daya fara to shi kawai zai karasa don yafi wannan din girma dakomai,idan yace zai cigaba dazama anan zai cigaba da tuna farida ne,gwara su fara sabuwar rayuwarsu shida Abu a sabon gida

Koda kaya suka isa gidansu Farida,jaraba da masifar  datayi Allah kadai yasan yawansu,bawanda ya kulata don lokacin babu kowa ma agidan,sai sauda haka tasha bakinciki ita kadai,"wato haka yusuf ya kagu yayi aure ya rabu da ita kenan?,dama ashe ya dade da tsanarta zaman gulma da munafurci kawai yake da ita yaki gaya mata har saida tagano don kanta,to inba haka ba wane irin abune wannan da bama zai iya jira tazo dakanta ba,daga yin abin jiya,shine zai kwashe mata komai ya aiko mata?wannan fa yana nuni dacewar ya tsaneta iya tsana kenan,da har baya kaunar yaga wani abu nata,hmm,to idan ma wai yana tunanin shikenan tadawo gida kenan dazama to kuwa zaisha mamaki,don itama nan bada dadewa ba zatayi aure ko ta halin kaka,don dolene ta muzguna mishi yafasan cewa bazatayi kwantai ba idan ya gaji da ita ya daina sonta akwai wayanda zasu karbeta hannu bibbiyu,ita har agaya mata farin jini ma,itada tun  tana budurwa ake rububinta har tayi aure baa daina yayinta ba,aikin banza ma kenan,tacigaba da mita
Batareda wani bata sauran lokaci ba yusuf ya tada ginin daya fara da yabari,don so yake ayi komai agama cikin kankanin lokaci babu wani amfanin ayi jinkiri Allah ya rufa mishi asiri
Soyayyarsu shida Abu kullum karuwa take,tabbas ta tabbatar yanzu tana sonshi kwarai da gaske,don tana zaune saitayita tunaninshi,musamman idan yadanyi jinkiri bai kirata ba ko ta kirashi bai dauka ba tayita damuwa kenan,idan hakan tafaru takan saka hotunanshi gaba tayita kallo( wayanda yasako mata awayar dawayanda yake tura  mata a watsapp don basuda aiki sai turawa juna hotuna tun tana jin kunya harta saba)tabbas sai yanzu  ta kara jin tausayin farida don ba karamin rashi tayiba,samun namiji irin yusuf abin sai an tona,don adan kwanakin nan da yusuf yake nuna mata tsantsar soyayya ta fuskanci wane irin  mutum ne shi ,zata iya cewa irin namijin nanne buri ko mafarkin   kowace ya mace amma farida duk ta watsar da hakan saboda tsananin yi wa kai da rashin rabo tabbas zatayi danasani
Kafin kuce meye wannan gini yayi nisa to harkace ta kudi,kuma duk step din  daaka dauka saiya tura mata  (Abu) tagani ko ya mata,dukda dai bata taba cewa wani abu bai mata ba don ita aganinta bata isa ba,amma hakan baisa yayi kasa agwiwa ba don ko tiles da penti saida ya tura mata hotuna akan tazaba taki kamar koda yaushe ganin ya nuna mata bacin ranshi ne yasa ta daure tazaba a karo na farko don ta faranta mishi,saboda yusuf ya mata komai bai cancanci bakantawa ba daga gareta ko da wasa,kuma duk abubuwan dake faruwa ganinsu take  kamar a mafarki wai yau ita Abu ce har ake nunawa ginin katafaren gida mai bene,ana cewa in ya mata,abinda yamata shi zaayi wanda bai mata ba a chanja,kai lallai rayuwa abin mamaki ce, yadda Allah yaso haka zaayi duk saurin mutum,dabara ko dagewar  mutum akan abu sai Allah ya nufa zai faru ita dai babu abinda take a kullum sai godewa Allah da wannan baiwa daya mata babu zato babu tsammani
Cikin kankanin lokaci aka hada lefe,na gani na fada,akwatuna goma sha shida yayi ganin yayi goma sha biyu lokacin farida kuma ya yasha alwashin saiya ninka  mata komai fiyeda  wanda yayi lokacin farida,don lokaci yariga yadade dayi da  mutanen duniya yakamata  su gane cewar wani kayan lefe dawani kyautatawa badole sai yayan masu kudi ba kawai,aa yayan talakawa ma zasu iya samun irin hakan,su samu sauyin rayuwa,duba da yadda lamuran duniyar nan suka zama na kwarya tabi kwarya,yayan masu kudi su auri junansu su kara wadata da daukaka, yayan talaka suma su auri junansu su kara talauci su dawwama a ciki,ayita rayuwa babu  sirki tayaya zaayi mu taba cigaba idan mukace zamu cigaba ahaka?
wannan dalilin ne ya karawa yusuf kaimi,don shi Allahn dayayi shi mutum ne maison kyautatawa baya kyamar talaka,yakuma kijinin yaga ana wulakantashi,tunda shima mutum ne dan Adam
Kafin kuce meye wannan,an gama shirya komai da komai,Tafiya kai kaya ma an  shirya dayake ma dai duk mazaa ne a harkar  babu mata,gudun gutsiri tsoma don babu abinda zai hana mutane yin magana,na farko dai  anhada wannan  uban kayan,na biyu,maiaiki wai zaa kaiwa kuma yar kauye,kunga kuwa ai abin magana ne dole,saidai idan anki gaskiya,to gudun hakan ne yasa Hajiya tace maza ne zasu kai asaka rana ayi komai a wuce wajen
motoci sukayi kusan nawa,shida bash ne agaba Amin yana bayan seat,suna tafe ana hira har aka karasa
Masu karatu kunsandai abinda zai faru  da zarar mutanen kauyensu Abu sunga  wayannan kaya, ko na fada adan rubutun nan ko ban fada ba,dolene ayi mamaki,da gulma ayi hassada ayi bakin ciki
su yusuf basu baro garin ba saida aka saka rana wata daya,koda baba yaji hakan kasa boye damuwarshi yayi don wannan babban tashin hankali ne zasu shiga ta ina zasu iya shirin biki nan da wata daya?Lura da hakan ne yasa daya daga cikin kawunnan yusuf din yace sudan kebe suyi magana,"wannan ba wani abin damuwa bane,don shi yusuf din yace in fada maka ya dauke muku komai"saurin dagowa baba yayi yana kallonshi cikeda mamaki,"yace baya bukatar komai daga wajenku,kun riga kun mai komai tunda kuka dauki ya kuka bashi,duk kayan dakin nan daakeyi dawasu tarkace duk bidia ne ba sunnah ba,don haka ka kwantar da hankalinka,kuma yace bayamaso kowa yasan cewa shi zaiyi komai din gudun gori da jahilcin mutane kasan halin jamaa
"kuka baba yasa don Abu ne dabai taba zata ba a duniya, suda hankalinsu in yayi dubu ya tashi don ta inda zai fitoda kudin kayan dakin nan ma tashin hankaline babba,ko da zaa bashi nan da shekara kuwa bazai iya hada kudinnan ba,to gashi Allah ya rufa musu asiri,wato haihuwa baiwa ce arziki na Allah ne,waye zaice Abu zata kawo musu irin  wannan arzikin ikon Allah yawane dashi
Ko da ya labartawa Dije itama sai da tayi nata na farinciki, don  yusuf yamusu komai,don koda ta fasa asusunta guda hudu data dade tana tara kudin sanaarta da niyyar idan auren Abu ya tashi a fasa ayi mata hidima, duka kudin ko dubu hamsin bai kaiba,hakan ne yasata shiga tashin hankali,da tunanin ta inda zata fara ciwo bashi,amma a halin yanzu babu abinda zasuyiwa Allah sai godiya tabbas
Yanmatan gari kuwa,duk wadda taji labari saita  garzayo ganin lefe don a kashe kwarkwatar ido,a tabbatar ko da gaskene,don dayawan mutane wayanda basuga kayan ba karyatawa suke,to abu ne dabaa  taba gani ba aagrin, sun saba amusu dan akwati  bityun su ko uku,to gwara ma su Laraba yar gidan maigari datafi  kowace yarinya  kyau da diri agarin itace aka mata akwati hudu lokacin aurenta da dan sarkin  kasuwa,aka dinga zuzutawa ana zance,to ashe basuga komai ba ga dai Abu yar gidan liman dakowa ya raina da akwatina goma sha shida,basusan gogan shi ashirin ma yayi niyyar yi ba don akan Abu zai iya komai shi kam, Hajiya ce tace yabar shi hakan idan tazo ayi mata duk abinda zaayi tunda dai tasan shi mai yin ne akwai kyautatawa
Harda makiyiyar dije kande,azuwa ganin lefe tsabagen gulma,bayan rabonta da gidan tun haihuwar Abun don tace gidan dije ai ba gidan zuwa bane tsiya tayi yawa baa harkar arziki,idankafiya zuwa ma saika shafi talauci,ba yadda baayi da ita ba ai akan karta auri malam liman babu irin shawarar dasu kawayenta basu bata ba akanshi,amma ta dage gashi nan ai,saboda tsananin talauci abu yayi abu har sun tura yarinya birni aikatau,(kuma fa kawar dijen  ce tun suna yara ganin ita mijinta yanada dan wadata ne irin tasu tacen yasata juyawa dijen baya yau kwananta biyu da dawowa daga cen birni taje suna,taji labarin lefe shine tabiyo sahu ta kashe kwarkwatar idanunta),mutanen duniya kenan ho!wato dai babu kunya ba tsoron Allah yau inbaka dashi ka shiga uku kai ba mutum bane bakada amfani, amma dazarar Allah  ya buda maka shikenan saika zama mai amfani mai muhimmanci  a idon mutane har ma sai ka fada aji don ka isa,hmm Allah ya sawwake
Gaisheta Abun tayi sannan ta shige daki tabasu waje,dayake dijen  batada riko bakuma tason  rigima ko biye mata batayi ba,da irin zantukan datake,don tasan abinda ya kawo ta,koda tagani kuwa hankalinta ne ya kara tashi,abu kamar amafarki,"kan uban cen!ji harkar arziki fisabilillahi,irin wayannan akwatuna? Ji kaya!oh ni kande"tace tareda rike haba,cikeda mamaki,tana zaxzaro ido,dan murmushi dije  tayi kawai,"tabarakallah mashaallah"tace, "lefen lawisa fa akwati biyu ya kawo mata shegen fakirin yaron nan dije"me ya kawo zancen lawisa kuma kande,yarinyar data kusa shekara da aure,kuma ai daidai karfinshi yayi dama zaki hada yaran mu na nan ne da na cen?"hmm matsiyaci sheg

Yayar  mahaifiyar Abu Gwaggo laure ce datazo ganin  kayan(sanda aka kawo bata nan)taga yadda ake suntiri agidan wai zuwa ganin lefe, ku kwace ma bikin ake,dama ita ba sauki batason hauka da rashin tunani,yar kauyece ita amma a wayen ta take,hade kan kayan tayi gabaki daya  tace akaisu dakin baba,ya isa haka,ai ba hauka bane abin,don wasu mutanen zuwansu nakusan nawa kenan,sai sun tafi sai wata tace ai don bakiga kaza  ba sai ace baa gani ba adawo,gashi ita dije bazata iya hanawa ba,kuma har wasu abubuwan sun fara bata,"da dai kinyi hakuri yaya,anbarsu kinsan yanzu sai ac
"ke wai yaushe zaki nutsu ne dije? zaunar da Abun tayi dakanta don ta lura dije fa dagaske take tsakaninta da Allah kunya takeji,bazata iya ba,dole yasa ita tadinga mata bayanin yadda zatayi amfanida komai,don  g lauren irin matan  nanne da babu ruwansu yan sabga,"kina wani sunkuyi dakai almura nasan ai kinsan komai yaran yanzu meye baku sani ba,zaki auri namijin daya taba aure yasan komai shine kuke zaune,to ni bazan bari ba,bazaayi haka dani ba bazai yiwuba  kije mishi haka atoh"ita dai abu sai sunkuyi dakai take  saboda kunya,don mahaifiyarta ta gada,ita abin ma mamaki  yake bata wato  dai da anyi zancen aure abinda  ake fara tunani kenan? to wai ita zama ta iya duk irin abubuwan datake karantawa a littatafai? gaskiya kunya takeji,"girki nasan  bakida matsala,tsabtar jiki da muhalli ma haka,sai kin  iya kissa Abu zama da miji saida haka,ki iya  tarairaya,zaki mallakeshi fiyeda tunaninki,ki kasance mai hakuri ladabi  da biyayyar damukasan ki dashi Abu don Allah don Annabi,karki chanja,"inshalalah zan kiyaye"tace kanta a kasa," matar dana karbo  kayannan wajenta tace tanada littatafai da idan kika karanta su zakifi ganewa anyi bayanin komai aciki da yadda zakiyi zaman auren shi kanshi,idan nakoma zan karbo su inshalalh,don Allah abu ki nutsu kada ki  bamu kunya kinji,kina dai ganin lamarin auren nan da yadda komai yafaru kamar amafarki,kicigaba da godewa Allah,kina addua baji ba gani abu,kinsandai makiya da mahassada sunyi yawa ko ina,kuma mijin nan naki har rabuwa yayi da matarshi saboda ke Abu don Allah don Annabi ki kasance mace tagari"inshaallah gwaggo zan kiyaye,nagode"tace
Ango yusuf anacen an gama gini daduk wani abu daya kamata,tabbas gida ya tsaru,don musamman ya dauko irin interior decorators dinnan sukayi aikinsu hakika komai ya tsaru yayi kyau,duk wani abu dakuka sani masu karatu da Iyaye suke kawo yarsu dashi yusuf yayi shi,tun daga kayan daki,kayan kujeru,kayan kitchen,har dinki yayi mata,saida yaje gida yana lissfawa Hajiya taji ko da abinda baiyi ba tace ai anayin su Humra su turaren wuta,bawani bata lokaci aka nemo wata wadda ta shahara ta kware,aka bata aiki

ai bata kai aya ba safina ta kwasheta  da wani wawan  mari,dama sun dade suna tara juna,"kai kai kai,kika mareni?ni na jawo kika dade agida kika kasa auruwa saboda bakin jini?"tace bayan   ta chakumeta,zantukan ta ne suka kara hasala safina  itama ta chakumeta ai sai kokawa,suka dinga bawa hammata iska,kowacce iya karfinta take cin uban yaruwarta,don duk awuya suke,lokacinyayi daidai  da fitowar mama daga kitchen ko kallonsu batayi  ba ta tabe baki tayi shigewarta daki don batada lokacin batawa,saida sukayi mai isarsu sannan kowacce tashiga daki tana huci cikeda bakincikin yaruwarta
"Shegiya mai bakiin jini ai wallahi kina nan saina sake aure  kina zaune,banza kawai,babbar asara"tace dakarfi bayan tabi safeenan dakinta,ta tarar ta shiga bandaki,"koda tadawo nata dakin key tasa ta rufe,don tasan tabbas bashi ta dauko,kwanciya tayi don duk abubuwan duniya su isheta,tunanin inda zata sami mijin aure,tafara,Mayenta ta tuno,tayi firgigit ta tashi zaune,taga ya sarara mata kwana biyu,ko meyasa oho?ko da yake ai tacimishi mutumci daidai gwargwado dole yayi zuciya,kai amma fa shi zaifi dacewa da ita,don yanada duk wani abu datake  bukata a tattare da miji tabbas yanzu ne lokacin dayafi dacewa  su gana,"gwara kawai ki nemoshi duk inda yake ki aureshi tunda dai shima yana sonki,dole ki nunawa safeena bata isa ba kuma batada wayo,yusuf yaji ajikinshi shima ya tabbatar bazakiyi kwantai ba
Gaskiya g
laure ba karamin kokari  take ba wajen ganin Abu ta kimtsu har gyaran jiki take mata dakanta don ta iya,su Abu anyi sumul anyi kyau,kamar ba ita ba
Duba datayi da Abu  batason shan abubuwan datake kawo mata ne yasa take zuwa musamman tasakata agaba  tasha tana gani,har wani turare ta kawo mata na wanka tun daga gashi har kafa ake wankewa dashi,ko sati batayi ba da fara amfani amma duk inda tayi sai ansan tazo donma Dai ba fita take ba,littattafan  kam takan  daure ta karanta don tana matukar son  karatu,dukda dai wasu abubuwan ma intana karantawa  ita kadai adaki kunya takeji,bare acecwai tayiwa miji tab,wai wanan wane irin lamari ne da zaace saita cire kunya lallai da aiki agabanta kenan

4
Rana bata karya,ayau aka daura auren Zainabu Abu da Yusuf a garinsu dake garin gumel,daurin auren da yasamu halaccin  manya manyan  mutane ba laifi tunda  baa gari bane,kuma yusuf babu wanda bai gayyata ba,hakika an halarta dayawa,don  tabbas mutane  sunyi mai kokari
Amarya  tasha  kyau dukda dai bawata kwalliya  datayi ba,amma dai gyaran jikin ya karbeta don tayi fes da ita,wani leshi ruwan kasa dayasha kayataccen dinki tasaka,da sarkar gwal wata tapkekiya(daya daga cikin ta kayan lefe)sai dan jambakinta data shafa,ta yafa mayafi abinta abin dai sai wanda yagani kowace mace dai da gaskiyar yusuf mai kyauce gyara kawai take bukata
Hakika anci  ansha  anyi hanian,don duk wani  abu na harkar abinci yusuf yasa anyi daga kano,kawai kaiwa akayi,ga hotuna daaka sha abin baa cewa komai
Ai Zuciyar farida bugawa ne kawai batayi ba dataga hoton daurin aure a instagram Wani shaharraren mai hoto yayi posting, don tunda  taga katin daurin aure,tayi  blocking kowa na yusuf a watsapp  dinta datasan zaiyi wani  update gameda biki harta gani ranta  ya sosu,to ashe ta gudu bata tsira ba,zatasha mamaki,"kutum
ta rapka wata ashar,wannan sarkar dai nasan ai ba ubanta bane ya siya shegiya yar talakawa"tace cikeda bakin cikin yadda sukayi kyau a hoton,"shegu jibesu, munafukan banza yarinya sai shegen baki,harda wani  rirrikemin  yaro (Amin)zaa mallakeshi a asirceshi yadda akayiwa ubanshi to ni nafi karfinki wallahi,baki isa  ba"tadinga maganganu  ita kadai kamar wadda tafara zaucewa, wani kuka  tafaashe dashi  cikeda takaici," to ke meye ma na kuka ne?ki karasa cireshi  daga zuciyarshi mana tunda gashi shi ya riga ya gama dake,ya tabbatar miki  dacewar duk abinki dai yazo kashe yayi aurenshi,ki manta dashi yadda yamanta dake wallahi yayi kadan yasaki cikin damuwa
Duk Abinda take mama na jinta,ranta kal don burinta Allah yanuna mata ranar dazasu nutsu su shiga hankalinsu su dawo hanya madaidaiciya,duk updates din da yusuf yake tana gani a status dinshi na watsapp don koda aka rabun ma yakan kirata lokaci zuwa lokaci su gaisa saboda yadda yake tsananin ganin girmanta kuma yasan batada laifi akan duk abubuwan dasuka faru
Tana zaune tana cigaba da zancen zuci cikeda bakin ciki ta shiga watsapp dinta mai zata gani,mama tayi updating status da Wannan hoton data gani,tarubuta Allah ya sanya Alkhairi Yabaku zaman lafiya,wayar tayi sauri ta kashe ta cillar gefe kar zuciyarta ta buga ,don tasan da gayya maman tayi haka itada sai tayi shekara batayi updating status ba,shine zata saka wannan hoton,bakomai tasan don tagani taji haushi ne amma bakomai nuna ma tagani ba
